{"type":"tool_use","timestamp":1782856861907,"sessionID":"ses_0e57366b4ffeVAMRD3KZD8mtXC","part":{"type":"tool","tool":"read","callID":"call_rmatfmsd","state":{"status":"completed","input":{"filePath":"/home/david/Code/vk-swarm/.claude/worktrees/bridge-cse_01B8B52jjMEdikaLRoA25qhr/docs/plans/vk-swarm-hive-redesign/CONTRACT.md"},"output":"<path>/home/david/Code/vk-swarm/.claude/worktrees/bridge-cse_01B8B52jjMEdikaLRoA25qhr/docs/plans/vk-swarm-hive-redesign/CONTRACT.md</path>\n<type>file</type>\n<content>\n1: # Cross-phase shared-interface contract — vk-swarm-hive-redesign (P2–P7)\n2: \n3: The single source of truth for interfaces that SPAN phases. Authored up front so dependent phases do\n4: not disagree on names/shapes (the parallel-authoring trap). Every Phase 2–7 task MUST conform; a task\n5: that needs to diverge STOPs and the divergence is recorded here first.\n6: \n7: ## A. WS message variants (hand-duplicated in BOTH crates — Trap 3)\n8: \n9: Defined identically in `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs` (node) AND\n10: `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs` (hive). Each new variant forces an arm in hive\n11: `handle_node_message` (`session.rs:512`, EXHAUSTIVE) and an EXPLICIT arm before the node `_ =>`\n12: wildcard (`hive_client.rs:1062`). **One protocol task per phase owns its variants; those tasks\n13: `conflicts_with` each other on the two enum files** (sequenced by depends_on, authored against this\n14: list so they never contradict).\n15: \n16: | Phase | Direction | Variant | Payload |\n17: |------|-----------|---------|---------|\n18: | P1 (done) | node→hive | `NodeMessage::OpBatch` | `{ ops: Vec<OutboxOp> }` |\n19: | P1 (done) | hive→node | `HiveMessage::OpAck` | `{ applied_through_seq: i64 }` |\n20: | P2 | node→hive | `NodeMessage::LeaseHeartbeat` | `{ assignment_ids: Vec<Uuid> }` |\n21: | P2 | hive→node | `HiveMessage::LeaseGrant` | `{ assignment_id: Uuid, fencing_token: i64, lease_expires_at: DateTime<Utc> }` |\n22: | P2 | hive→node | `HiveMessage::LeaseRevoked` | `{ assignment_id: Uuid, reason: String }` |\n23: | P5 | node→hive | `NodeMessage::Digest` | `{ entries: Vec<DigestEntry> }` (DigestEntry `{ entity_type: String, entity_id: Uuid, version: i64 }`) |\n24: | P5 | hive→node | `HiveMessage::DigestResult` | `{ resend_from_seq: Option<i64>, pull_entities: Vec<Uuid> }` |\n25: \n26: P3 (status) and P4 (inbound collapse) add **no** new WS variant — status rides the P1 op-log\n27: (`task.upsert` carries status, gated by the P3 matrix); P4 changes inbound apply semantics, not the\n28: wire.\n29: \n30: ## B. Schema additions\n31: \n32: | Phase | DB | Change |\n33: |------|----|--------|\n34: | P2 | Postgres (hive) | `ALTER TABLE node_task_assignments ADD COLUMN lease_expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ, ADD COLUMN fencing_token BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`; a monotonic token source — `CREATE SEQUENCE node_fencing_token_seq` (per-hive monotonic; the grant does `nextval`). |\n35: | P7 | Postgres (hive) | one-time cutover migration(s) per ADR-0011 (migrate / regenerate / discard); preserves the `shared_task_id ↔ source_task_id` id bridge; remaps status enum values. |\n36: \n37: No node-SQLite schema change beyond P1's `node_outbox` (its `fencing_token INTEGER` column already\n38: exists for P2 to populate).\n39: \n40: ## C. Fencing semantics (P2, consumed by P3/P6)\n41: \n42: - The node stamps `OutboxOp.fencing_token` (P1 column) **only for ops against a hive-assigned task**;\n43:   node-owned work leaves it `NULL` (ADR-0009 scope). The hive `handle_op_batch` (106) gains a fencing\n44:   check: for an op whose task has an active assignment, **reject (skip, do NOT apply, do NOT advance\n45:   high-water past a rejected op — return an error/`LeaseRevoked`) if `op.fencing_token < assignment.fencing_token`**.\n46: - Node self-fence: a renew-deadline watchdog halts the agent (reuse ADR-0001 process-group fence) when\n47:   a lease cannot be renewed within its TTL.\n48: - Lease-expiry sweep: a hive timer (analog of `crates/remote/src/services/stale_cleanup.rs`) reclaims\n49:   assignments whose `lease_expires_at < now()`, bumping `fencing_token = nextval(...)`.\n50: \n51: ## D. Status state machine (P3, ADR-0010) — RECONCILED to the real enum (ratified 2026-06-30)\n52: \n53: `task.status` ∈ `{Todo, InProgress, InReview, Done, Cancelled}` (both crates) — there is **no\n54: `Assigned`/`Failed` variant**. SC4's `assigned`/`failed` are authority LABELS, not status values:\n55: `assigned` = an active `node_task_assignments` row (hive, assignment layer); `failed` = an\n56: `execution_status` outcome (node, execution layer). The **`task.status` single-author matrix**:\n57: - **Hive-authored:** `todo→in-progress` (assign+start), `in-review→done`/`in-review→in-progress`\n58:   (operator review), `*→cancelled`.\n59: - **Node-reported** (only with a valid lease + current fencing token, CONTRACT §C):\n60:   `in-progress→in-review`, `in-progress→done`.\n61: \n62: One canonical wire value (node lowercase `inprogress`/`inreview` ↔ hive `in-progress`/`in-review` — the\n63: mapping P1/106-F5 pins). See ADR-0010 for the full reconciliation rationale.\n64: \n65: ## E. Inbound single channel (P4, ADR-0007)\n66: \n67: WS activity stream = single live inbound channel; bulk snapshot demoted to cold-start/gap-fill reconcile\n68: only; the dead `ElectricTaskSyncService` task-shape path removed. One delete semantic = soft-unlink +\n69: tombstone (clear `shared_task_id`, keep local `task_attempt`), identical on both legs. Node dirty-guard:\n70: an inbound update never overwrites a field with an unacked outbound op. Handle `task.reassigned`\n71: (`processor.rs:77` gap).\n72: \n73: ## F. No-fanout (P6, ADR-0007 data plane) — verify+guard\n74: \n75: Investigation found the node-facing channel already carries only `ProjectSync`/`NodeRemoved` (NOT shared\n76: task state). P6 = a test/guard asserting the invariant + a comment fence; NOT a large removal. Authored up front so dependent phases do\nnot disagree on names/shapes (the parallel-authoring trap). Every Phase 2–7 task MUST conform; a task\nthat needs to diverge STOPs and the divergence is recorded here first.\n\n## A. WS message variants (hand-duplicated in BOTH crates — Trap 3)\n\nDefined identically in `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs` (node) AND\n`crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs` (hive). Authored up front so dependent phases do\nnot disagree on names/shapes (the parallel-authoring trap). Every Phase 2–7 task MUST conform; a task\nthat needs to diverge STOPs and the divergence is recorded here first.\n\n## A. WS message variants (hand-duplicated in BOTH crates — Trap 3)\n\nDefined identically in `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs` (node) AND\n`crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs` (hive). Each new variant forces an arm in hive\n`handle_node_message` (`session.rs:512`, EXHAUSTIVE) and an EXPLICIT arm before the node `_ =>`\nwildcard (`hive_client.rs:1062`). **One protocol task per phase owns its variants; those tasks\n`conflicts_with` each other on the two enum files** (sequenced by depends_on, authored against this\nlist so they never contradict).\n\n| Phase | Direction | Variant | Payload |\n|------|-----------|---------|---------|\n| P1 (done) | node→hive | `NodeMessage::OpBatch` | `{ ops: Vec<OutboxOp> }` |\n| P1 (done) | hive→node | `HiveMessage::OpAck` | `{ applied_through_seq: i64 }` |\n| P2 | node→hive | `NodeMessage::LeaseHeartbeat` | `{ assignment_ids: Vec<Uuid> }` |\n| P2 | hive→node | `HiveMessage::LeaseGrant` | `{ assignment_id: Uuid, fencing_token: i64, lease_expires_at: DateTime<Utc> }` |\n| P2 | hive→node | `HiveMessage::LeaseRevoked` | `{ assignment_id: Uuid, reason: String }` |\n| P5 | node→hive | `NodeMessage::Digest` | `{ entries: Vec<DigestEntry> }` (DigestEntry `{ entity_type: String, entity_id: Uuid, version: i64 }`) |\n| P5 | hive→node | `HiveMessage::DigestResult` | `{ resend_from_seq: Option<i64>, pull_entities: Vec<Uuid> }` |\n\nP3 (status) and P4 (inbound collapse) add **no** new WS variant — status rides the P1 op-log\n(`task.upsert` carries status, gated by the P3 matrix); P4 changes inbound apply semantics, not the\nwire.\n\n## B. Schema additions\n\n| Phase | DB | Change |\n|------|----|--------|\n| P2 | Postgres (hive) | `ALTER TABLE node_task_assignments ADD COLUMN lease_expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ, ADD COLUMN fencing_token BIGINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0`; a monotonic token source — `CREATE SEQUENCE node_fencing_token_seq` (per-hive monotonic; the grant does `nextval`). |\n| P7 | Postgres (hive) | one-time cutover migration(s) per ADR-0011 (migrate / regenerate / discard); preserves the `shared_task_id ↔ source_task_id` id bridge; remaps status enum values. |\n\nNo node-SQLite schema change beyond P1's `node_outbox` (its `fencing_token INTEGER` column already\nexists for P2 to populate).\n\n## C. Fencing semantics (P2, consumed by P3/P6)\n\n- The node stamps `OutboxOp.fencing_token` (P1 column) **only for ops against a hive-assigned task**;\n  node-owned work leaves it `NULL` (ADR-0009 scope). The hive `handle_op_batch` (106) gains a fencing\n  check: for an op whose task has an active assignment, **reject (skip, do NOT apply, do NOT advance\n  high-water past a rejected op — return an error/`LeaseRevoked`) if `op.fencing_token < assignment.fencing_token`**.\n- Node self-fence: a renew-deadline watchdog halts the agent (reuse ADR-0001 process-group fence) when\n  a lease cannot be renewed within its TTL.\n- Lease-expiry sweep: a hive timer (analog of `crates/remote/src/services/stale_cleanup.rs`) reclaims\n  assignments whose `lease_expires_at < now()`, bumping `fencing_token = nextval(...)`.\n\n## D. Status state machine (P3, ADR-0010) — RECONCILED to the real enum (ratified 2026-06-30)\n\n`task.status` ∈ `{Todo, InProgress, InReview, Done, Cancelled}` (both crates) — there is **no\n`Assigned`/`Failed` variant**. SC4's `assigned`/`failed` are authority LABELS, not status values:\n`assigned` = an active `node_task_assignments` row (hive, assignment layer); `failed` = an\n`execution_status` outcome (node, execution layer). The **`task.status` single-author matrix**:\n- **Hive-authored:** `todo→in-progress` (assign+start), `in-review→done`/`in-review→in-progress`\n  (operator review), `*→cancelled`.\n- **Node-reported** (only with a valid lease + current fencing token, CONTRACT §C):\n  `in-progress→in-review`, `in-progress→done`.\n\nOne canonical wire value (node lowercase `inprogress`/`inreview` ↔ hive `in-progress`/`in-review` — the\nmapping P1/106-F5 pins). See ADR-0010 for the full reconciliation rationale.\n\n## E. Inbound single channel (P4, ADR-0007)\n\nWS activity stream = single live inbound channel; bulk snapshot demoted to cold-start/gap-fill reconcile\nonly; the dead `ElectricTaskSyncService` task-shape path removed. One delete semantic = soft-unlink +\ntombstone (clear `shared_task_id`, keep local `task_attempt`), identical on both legs. Node dirty-guard:\nan inbound update never overwrites a field with an unacked outbound op. Handle `task.reassigned`\n(`processor.rs:77` gap).\n\n## F. No-fanout (P6, ADR-0007 data plane) — verify+guard\n\nInvestigation found the node-facing channel already carries only `ProjectSync`/`NodeRemoved` (NOT shared\ntask state). P6 = a test/guard asserting the invariant + a comment fence; NOT a large removal. Browser\nfan-out (`electric_proxy`/`ActivityBroker`) is OUT of scope (hive-UI data source).","lineStart":1,"lineEnd":77,"totalLines":77,"truncated":false}},"title":"docs/plans/vk-swarm-hive-redesign/CONTRACT.md","time":{"start":1782856861901,"end":1782856861906}},"id":"prt_f1a8cc8ca001TpLu3zXoEt0awc","sessionID":"ses_0e57366b4ffeVAMRD3KZD8mtXC","messageID":"msg_f1a8cc33f002Zm5NEAelAKgPaj"}}

Pre-empted traps for implementers are\n9: added at decompose time.\n10: \n11: ## Pre-empted traps (read before executing ANY task)\n12: \n13: Carried forward from `vk-swarm-node-foundations` (same repo, same gate) + hive/Postgres analogues. The\n14: node-foundations ledger is the authority for the originals; condensed here.\n15: \n16: ### Trap 1 — WAI gate is TypeScript-shaped; this is a Cargo workspace\n17: Every Rust task sets BOTH in its `## Done when`: `WAI_TYPECHECK_CMD=\"cargo check -p <crate>\"` (or\n18: `--workspace` when arms span crates) and `WAI_TEST_CMD=\"cargo test -p <crate> <test_name>\"`. Omitting\n19: them runs the wrong/no check — a hollow pass.\n20: \n21: ### Trap 2 — SQLx OFFLINE on the node (SQLite) side; build against a live migrated DB\n22: Committed `.sqlx` cache + unset `DATABASE_URL` → `query!` validates against the cache, not a live DB.\n23: Tasks adding a migration + new query export `DATABASE_URL=sqlite://<repo>/dev_assets/db.sqlite` against\n24: a migrated dev DB. **Never run `cargo sqlx prepare` in a gated task** (it rewrites tracked `.sqlx/*.json`\n25: the gate's file-allow-list rejects). Regenerate once at `/wai:close`.\n26: \n27: ### Trap 2b — Hive (Postgres / `crates/remote`) query validation + tests need a LIVE Postgres (confirmed)\n28: Confirmed in code: the remote crate's `query!`/`query_as!` validate against the **shared root `.sqlx`\n29: offline cache** (same cache as the node side). Adding/changing a Postgres query therefore needs a live\n30: `DATABASE_URL`/`SERVER_DATABASE_URL` pointed at a **migrated Postgres** (`crates/remote/src/config.rs:45`)\n31: OR a cache regen — it will NOT validate against the SQLite dev DB. **And hive integration tests SKIP\n32: without a DB:** `crates/remote/tests/backfill_e2e.rs` uses `skip_without_db!` (returns early if\n33: `DATABASE_URL` unset); the hermetic SQLite `db::test_utils::create_test_pool()` does **not** apply to\n34: the hive. **Consequence for every hive-side task (102, 107, and all of P2/P3/P6/P7 hive work):** its\n35: `scope_test` is a `#[tokio::test]` that REQUIRES `DATABASE_URL=postgres://…` against a migrated PG, or\n36: the WAI gate runs a SKIPPED test and reports a **hollow pass**. The executor MUST stand up a Postgres\n37: (migrated via `sqlx::migrate!(\"./migrations\")`, `crates/remote/src/db/mod.rs:51`) and export\n38: `DATABASE_URL` before running any hive task. A hive task with no Postgres precondition + a skip-guarded\n39: test is NOT verifiable — flag such tasks. (This is genuinely harder than node-foundations, which never\n40: touched the remote crate. If a CI Postgres is not readily available, raise it before executing P-hive\n41: tasks.)\n42: \n43: ### Trap 3 — `enum_dispatch` / WS-message exhaustiveness on BOTH ends\n44: Adding a `NodeMessage` or `ServerMessage` variant (op-log op, durable ack, heartbeat, lease grant)\n45: forces editing **every** match arm on that end in the SAME commit or the workspace won't compile under\n46: `-D warnings`. The node side (`hive_client.rs`/`hive_sync.rs`/`node_runner.rs`) AND the hive side\n47: (`crates/remote` WS dispatch) each have their own exhaustive match sites — a new variant is a single\n48: cohesive `mixed` task per end (or one cross-cutting task), not a create+wire split. Anchor list of arms\n49: is filled from the hive-side anchor investigation.\n50: \n51: ### Trap 4 — Know which crate owns the logic (no cross-crate inversion)\n52: `services` does not depend on `local-deployment`; trait methods dispatch into the impl. Confirm the\n53: owning crate/trait for each touched function before authoring (the node-foundations recovery work lived\n54: in the `services` trait, not `local-deployment`). For hive logic, confirm `crates/remote` ownership.\n55: \n56: ### Trap 5 — Anchor-checker strips `crates/*/` (precheck false-positive) — already hit\n57: See Precheck notes below. Recorded so a precheck re-run is not mistaken for a real contradiction.\n58: \n59: ### Trap 6 — Frozen spec; escalate scope discoveries to the user\n60: The spec is frozen at precheck (ADR-0001). A spec-vs-reality contradiction or an entangled/oversized\n61: area discovered during decompose is **escalated to the user**, never papered over with a vague task or\n62: a silent spec edit — exactly how node-foundations carved out `vk-swarm-node-ui-localize`. The SC1\n63: central-UI carve (see plan Scope note) follows this protocol.\n64: \n65: ## Decompose decisions (2026-06-30)\n66: \n67: ### USER-APPROVED SCOPE SPLIT — SC1 central-management UI → `vk-swarm-hive-ui`\n68: Decompose found SC1 has two separable halves: (a) the **data-plane** guarantee \"no node↔node /\n69: node↔hive↔node fan-out\", and (b) the **hive web UI manages all** cross-node tasks/attempts/executions.\n70: Half (b) is a workstream-scale frontend build (the hive UI today is a 4-page auth stub; the\n71: management UI lives in the *node* frontend; cross-node task/attempt/execution views are net-new). **User\n72: decision (2026-06-30): carve half (b) into `vk-swarm-hive-ui`** (tracker seeded, no spec yet). This\n73: workstream covers SC2–SC7 + SC1's data-plane half (phase-6). SC1 stays in the frozen spec, claimed by\n74: phase-6; the UI deferral is recorded here — **no spec edit** (mirrors the node-foundations →\n75: `vk-swarm-node-ui-localize` carve).\n76: \n77: ### Finding — SC1 \"no fan-out of shared task state\" is LARGELY ALREADY SATISFIED\n78: Verified in code: the hive's node-facing broadcast (`ConnectionManager::send_to_nodes`/`broadcast_to_org`,\n79: `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs:138,189`) carries **only** `ProjectSync` and `NodeRemoved` —\n80: it does **not** push shared-*task* state to nodes today. The shared-task fan-out that exists\n81: (`electric_proxy.rs` `GET /v1/shape/shared_tasks` + `ActivityBroker`, `crates/remote/src/activity/broker.rs:48`)\n82: targets **browsers** (which the hive UI needs). **Therefore phase-6 (SC1 data-plane) is \"verify + guard\n83: against regression + keep the node-facing channel assignment-only,\" not \"remove a large fan-out.\"** This\n84: is surfaced (not a contradiction): SC1's data-plane intent is met by construction; the task asserts and\n85: fences it. Browser-facing fan-out (electric_proxy/broker) is OUT of scope for \"no fan-out\" — it is the\n86: hive-UI data source.\n87: \n88: ### Decompose decision — WS protocol enums are hand-duplicated; DUAL-EDIT, do not deduplicate (this workstream)\n89: `NodeMessage`/`HiveMessage` are defined **twice** — hive `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs:15,91`\n90: and node `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs:82,123` — and have **already drifted** (`Deregister`\n91: exists hive-side only). Every new variant (op-log op, durable ack, heartbeat, lease grant) is added to\n92: **both** copies in the same commit (Trap 3). **Decision:** keep the dual-definition convention and add\n93: variants to both — deduplicating into a shared protocol crate is hygiene OUT of scope here (it would be\n94: a large cross-crate move touching every match site). Each protocol task is a single cohesive `mixed`\n95: task editing both crates + the exhaustive hive match (`session.rs:512`) + an explicit node arm **before\n96: the `_ =>` wildcard at `hive_client.rs:1062`** (the wildcard silently drops unhandled hive→node variants\n97: — the #1 easy-to-miss bug here).\n98: \n99: ### Decompose decision — durable-ack emission requires threading `ws_sender` into apply handlers\n100: Hive apply handlers `handle_attempt_sync`/`handle_execution_sync`/`handle_logs_batch`\n101: (`session.rs:1188,1307,1388`) currently take `node_id`/`pool` only — **not** the WS sender. Emitting a\n102: durable per-op ack (the SC2c fix) requires threading `ws_sender` into those signatures. `handle_task_sync`\n103: (session.rs:1547, replies `TaskSyncResponse`) and `handle_heartbeat` (replies `HeartbeatAck`,\n104: session.rs:607) are the existing templates. The op-log apply is a NEW `handle_op_batch` handler beside\n105: them; acks reuse the `HeartbeatAck` send shape.\n106: \n107: ### Decompose decision — PHASE-BY-PHASE authoring (user-approved)\n108: This decompose authors **Phase 1 (the op-log foundation) only**; later phases are authored in subsequent\n109: `/wai:decompose` passes as each prior ships (user decision 2026-06-30). Consequence for the gate:\n110: `wai-plan-lint` reads ALL spec SC ids from the token and will report SC1,SC3–SC7 **unclaimed** until\n111: their phases are authored — this is **expected-pending**, not a lint failure to paper over. Phase 1's\n112: internal consistency (plan↔frontmatter deps/conflicts, verification present, failing-tests-first) IS\n113: enforced now. A full PLAN-LINT PASS is achieved only when the final phase is authored.\n114: \n115: ## Phase-1 authoring — ratified judgment calls + tracer limitations (2026-06-30)\n116: \n117: The Phase-1 author surfaced six judgment calls (Trap 6). Ratified after review:\n118: \n119: 1. **106 parks on project-link-absent, not parent-task-absent** — RATIFIED. `upsert_from_node`\n120:    (`tasks.rs:566`) has no parent-task FK; the real transient dependency is the ProjectsSync link, which\n121:    `handle_task_sync` already encodes. Correct reading of SC2b at the task tier.\n122: 2. **106 splits PARK (transient, `node_local_projects` row absent) vs SKIP+ADVANCE (permanent,\n123:    not swarm-linked)** — RATIFIED, and load-bearing. Because 105 enqueues for ALL projects (the `db`\n124:    crate can't cheaply do the swarm lookup), a non-swarm task at the outbox head would park *permanently*\n125:    and wedge the cursor if \"not linked\" parked. The split (encoded as 106's third test) prevents the\n126:    wedge. This mirrors `handle_task_sync`'s three-branch resolution.\n127: 3. **105 idempotency_key = `task:{id}:{uuid}` (per-write-unique, persisted on the op row), NOT\n128:    `task:{id}:{version}`** — RATIFIED. `Task::update` (`queries.rs:305`) bumps no version, so a\n129:    version-key would self-collide and `UNIQUE(idempotency_key)` would silently drop updates. A re-sent\n130:    op reuses its stored key → hive dedups. (Same no-version fact as ADR-0007's dirty-guard motivation.)\n131: 4. **105 enqueue is best-effort, non-atomic** with the task write (callers hold `&SqlitePool`, not a\n132:    txn) — RATIFIED as a TRACER LIMITATION. The legacy sync path is the backstop. **Consequence:\n133:    Phase-1-tracer does NOT fully satisfy SC2c \"zero silent write loss\" — true no-loss needs the enqueue\n134:    in the SAME transaction as the entity write** (threading a txn through the ~8 `Task::create` callers),\n135:    which is the next Phase-1 increment. SC2c is *claimed* by 102/106/108 (the durable-ack mechanism) but\n136:    the no-loss guarantee is only fully closed by the transactional enqueue.\n137: 5. **108 advances the cursor via a new `HiveEvent::OpAck`** consumed in `run_node_runner` (which holds\n138:    the pool), mirroring the `TaskSyncResponse`/`BackfillRequest` \"DB write happens in run_node_runner\"\n139:    pattern — RATIFIED. `HiveEvent` has no third/cross-crate match site (grep-verified), so 108's `files:`\n140:    (hive_client.rs + node_runner.rs) is complete.\n141: 6. **Trap 2b (Postgres) applies to 102 + 106** — RATIFIED; each states the live-PG precondition.\n142: \n143: **Honest SC2 status after Phase-1-tracer:** the ordered, acknowledged round-trip *mechanism* is proven\n144: (SC2a single ordered channel — additive, alongside legacy; SC2b parent/link-before-child parking; SC2c\n145: durable per-op ack + cursor-advance-only-on-ack). NOT yet done: transactional enqueue (full SC2c\n146: no-loss), attempt/exec/log op types, and retirement of the five legacy push paths. These are tracked as\n147: the next Phase-1 increment in plan.md.\n148: \n149: ## Phase-1 sibling-advisory acknowledgement (wai-plan-lint `W:` lines, SC6)\n150: \n151: - **101 `…_add_node_outbox.sql` beside `…_init.sql`** — migrations are independent forward-only DDL, NOT\n152:   reimplementations of a pattern. Authored to house conventions confirmed against the recent\n153:   `queued_messages` migration (BLOB UUID PKs, `datetime('now','subsec')`, `CREATE … IF NOT EXISTS`,\n154:   partial index). Not a pattern sibling.\n155: - **102 `…_add_node_op_log.sql` beside `…_shared_tasks_activity.sql`** — same: independent Postgres DDL,\n156:   not a pattern sibling. **102's test `node_op_log_migration.rs` beside `backfill_e2e.rs` IS a real\n157:   sibling** — the task reads it and reuses its `database_url()`/`skip_without_db!`/`create_pool()`\n158:   helpers verbatim (no shared `common` module exists). Acknowledged, handled in-task.\n159: - **104 `node_outbox.rs` beside `activity_dismissal.rs`** — the task carries a `## Sibling alignment`\n160:   step reading an existing `db` model (`draft.rs`) for trait surface / error type / test style. The\n161:   genuine pattern sibling is read; `activity_dismissal.rs` is one of many same-dir models, not the\n162:   authority. Acknowledged.\n163: \n164: ## Phase-1 lint status (expected-pending, not a failure to paper over)\n165: After the Phase-1 fixes (SC2/TS1 claimed; clause sub-ids SC2a/b/c are colon-less PROSE in the spec so\n166: the lint's declared id is `SC2`), `wai-plan-lint` reports only **SC1, SC3–SC7 and TS2–TS7 unclaimed** —\n167: the unauthored phases. This is the documented phase-by-phase state; a full PLAN-LINT PASS lands when the\n168: final phase is authored. Phase-1 internal consistency (deps/conflicts ↔ frontmatter, verification\n169: present, failing-tests-first) passes.\n170: \n171: ## Phase-6 authoring — no-fanout VERIFY+GUARD (2026-06-30)\n172: \n173: Phase-6 (SC1 data-plane) authored as a small verify+guard, per the plan/CONTRACT §F. Re-verified the\n174: current no-fanout state directly before authoring; the invariant **HOLDS** — see findings below.\n175: \n176: ### Re-verification — every hive→node send site enumerated (the no-fanout state confirmed)\n177: `grep \"HiveMessage::\"` across `crates/remote/src` + the four send primitives in `connection.rs`\n178: (`send_to_node`@123, `broadcast_to_org`@138, `broadcast_to_org_except`@159, `send_to_nodes`@189) yields\n179: the COMPLETE hive→node send inventory:\n180: - `ProjectSync` (session.rs:856/994/1859 via `send_to_nodes`/`broadcast_to_org`) — project METADATA\n181:   (link id, repo path, branch, owner-node display), NOT shared-task state. Targeted to linked nodes.\n182: - `NodeRemoved` (session.rs:1087 via `broadcast_to_org`) — node-lifecycle control.\n183: - `TaskAssign` (dispatcher.rs:103/252 via `send_to_node`) — sent ONLY to the **target/owning** node;\n184:   it IS that node's OWN assignment, NOT relay of another node's state. (Task-shaped, but not fan-out.)\n185: - `BackfillRequest` (backfill.rs:188/257 via `send_to_node`) — a request for the recipient to push ITS\n186:   OWN data up; carries no task state.\n187: - `AuthResult`/`Close`/`HeartbeatAck`/`TaskSyncResponse`/`Error`/`StatusRequest` (session.rs, via the\n188:   socket sink `send_message`, not the broadcast primitives) — per-node handshake/control/ack replies on\n189:   the recipient's OWN socket.\n190: - `LabelSync` (broadcast variant) — declared in `HiveMessage` but **never constructed/sent** today (the\n191:   inbound `NodeMessage::LabelSync` handler ignores it; session.rs:543/1536). Classified as `LabelMetadata`\n192:   defensively; even if sent it is org-global label metadata, not task state.\n193: - `TaskCancel` — constructed ONLY in a commented-out TODO (dispatcher.rs:189-194); never sent.\n194: **Conclusion (no finding):** no `HiveMessage` the hive delivers to a node pushes another node's shared-\n195: *task* state to a third node. SC1's data-plane intent is met by construction; phase-6 asserts + fences it.\n196: \n197: ### Judgment call — anchor list in the task brief was a SUBSET; the guard covers ALL send variants\n198: The brief's anchors named ProjectSync@889/1021/1873 + NodeRemoved@1096 as the call sites. The full\n199: inventory above also includes `TaskAssign` (dispatcher) and `BackfillRequest` (backfill.rs) sent via\n200: `send_to_node`, plus the per-node `send_message` replies. These are NOT fan-out of foreign task state\n201: (own-assignment / own-backfill / per-node control), so they do not contradict §F — but the 601 guard\n202: classifies **every** `HiveMessage` variant exhaustively (not just the two ProjectSync/NodeRemoved\n203: broadcast payloads), which is strictly stronger and future-proof. Recorded so a reviewer expecting only\n204: the two named variants understands the guard's wider, deliberate scope.\n205: \n206: ### Judgment call — HERMETIC test (no Postgres); Trap 2b deliberately NOT invoked\n207: 601 is a pure static/enum guard over `HiveMessage` — no `query!`, no socket, no DB. Per the brief\n208: (\"a pure enum/static guard test may be hermetic — prefer that\"), it is a plain `crates/remote/tests/`\n209: integration test importing `vks_hive_server::nodes::ws::message::HiveMessage` (all `pub`). It has **no**\n210: `DATABASE_URL` precondition and **no** `skip_without_db!` — so it can never report a hollow skip-pass.\n211: This is the one phase-6 task that escapes Trap 2b (it touches no Postgres query). Gate uses the Rust\n212: overrides (Trap 1): `cargo check -p vks-hive-server --tests` + `cargo test --test no_fanout_invariant`.\n213: \n214: ### Judgment call — 2 tasks: `create` guard (601) + comment-only `edit` fence (602)\n215: Split to keep `allowed_change` clean: 601 is `create` (new test file, the executable invariant); 602 is\n216: a comment-only `edit` to the SHARED file `connection.rs` (the documented regression fence at the send\n217: sites, pointing future authors at the 601 test). 602 `depends_on` 601 (the comment references the test).\n218: 602 has `scope_test: N/A` + a `## Manual verification` section (comment-only; no behavior to unit-test) —\n219: schema-valid. **SHARED FILE NOTE:** 602 touches `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs`, also the\n220: home of the `send_to_node`/`broadcast_to_org`/`send_to_nodes` primitives that later phases (P2 lease,\n221: P3 status) read but do not modify; 602's edit is the module doc-comment only (no signature/behavior\n222: change), so it does not conflict with any P1/P2/P3 task — `conflicts_with: []` is correct.\n223: \n224: ### Judgment call — 602 claims NO `covers_criteria`/`covers_tests` (601 fully claims SC1+TS7)\n225: 602 is a comment-only `edit` to a CODE file (`connection.rs`). `wai-plan-lint`'s SC6 rule fires for any\n226: `create|mixed|edit` task with a non-empty `covers_criteria` AND ≥1 code file, REQUIRING a non-empty\n227: `## Failing test (write first)` free of `N/A`/deferral keywords; the doc-only carve-out applies only when\n228: ALL `files:` are `.md/.mdx/.json/.toml/.yaml/.yml` — which a `.rs` edit is not. A comment fence has no\n229: failing test to write. **Resolution:** 602 carries `covers_criteria: []` and `covers_tests: []` — SC1 and\n230: TS7 are fully claimed by **601** (which DOES write the failing test). 602 is a supporting documentation\n231: fence, not an SC-claiming task; this satisfies the lint and is the honest reading.\n232: \n233: ### Judgment call — fence centralized at `connection.rs` (the four send primitives), NOT `session.rs`\n234: The brief named both files as send sites. EVERY hive→node push funnels through the four `ConnectionManager`\n235: primitives in `connection.rs` (`send_to_node`/`broadcast_to_org`/`broadcast_to_org_except`/`send_to_nodes`);\n236: `session.rs`'s `send_message` is the per-node socket-sink reply path for handshake/control/ack\n237: (auth_result/close/heartbeat_ack/task_sync_response) — NOT a broadcast/relay path, so it cannot fan out\n238: another node's task state by construction. The 602 comment fence sits ONLY at `connection.rs` (the choke\n239: point; lower-conflict, doc-comment only); **601's exhaustive `HiveMessage` guard covers the\n240: `session.rs`-delivered variants too** (it classifies ALL variants regardless of sending primitive). The\n241: `session.rs` omission is intentional.\n242: \n243: ### Judgment call — ENUM-DRIFT fence: 601 anticipates the GROWN `HiveMessage` (P6 runs after P1/P2/P5)\n244: 601's `classify` is an EXHAUSTIVE match over `HiveMessage`; P6 is sequenced after P1/P2/P5, which ADD\n245: hive→node variants (CONTRACT §A: `OpAck`@P1-task-103, `LeaseGrant`/`LeaseRevoked`@P2,\n246: `DigestResult`@P5-task-501). Against main's 12-variant enum the authored match goes NON-exhaustive once\n247: those land → compile error → gate fail, leaving the executor to classify them by judgment (the exact drift\n248: WAI decision-locking prevents). **Fixes:** (1) 601 `depends_on: [\"103\"]` (plan row `dep: 103` for lint\n249: equality) — the authored variant-adding task; 601's test code already includes the\n250: `OpAck { applied_through_seq }` arm + constructor (guaranteed via the dep), classified `PerNodeControl`.\n251: (2) A DECISION-LOCKED table in 601's body fixes `LeaseGrant`/`LeaseRevoked`→`OwnAssignment`,\n252: `DigestResult`→`PerNodeControl` (all struct-variants `{ .. }` per §A; `DigestResult` confirmed against 501)\n253: — the executor APPLIES the rule, never judges. None is foreign-task-state fan-out, so the assertion holds.\n254: P2/P5 are NOT hard task-id deps (their ids aren't authored yet; the spine ordering is prose) — the\n255: decision-locked table + commented arms cover them when they land.\n256: \n257: ### Lint note (expected-pending) — SC1 + TS7 CLAIMED by phase-6 (601)\n258: With phase-6 authored, `wai-plan-lint` SC1 moves unclaimed → claimed by **601** (`covers_criteria: [SC1]`,\n259: `covers_tests: [TS7]`); 602 claims neither. Remaining unclaimed ids are the still-unauthored phases\n260: (2,3,4,7 → SC3/SC4/SC7/SC6 + TS2/TS3/TS5/TS6; P5 authored separately) — the phase-by-phase state, not a\n261: failure.\n262: \n263: ## Phase-5 authoring — anti-entropy digest, SC5/TS4 (2026-06-30)\n264: \n265: Phase-5 (anti-entropy reconciliation digest) authored as four tasks (501–504) riding P1's op-log per\n266: ADR-0008 §\"Anti-entropy reconciliation (SC5)\" + CONTRACT §A. Mirrors P1's 103/107/106/108 shape\n267: (protocol variants / node emit / hive apply+reply / node act). Judgment calls below were ratified before\n268: authoring (advisor-reviewed).\n269: \n270: ### CONTRACT §A shapes are FIXED — digest carries NO hash, NO outbox high-water field\n271: The brief's prose (\"per-entity version/hash + outbox high-water\") is WIDER than CONTRACT §A's frozen\n272: shapes: `DigestEntry = { entity_type, entity_id, version }` (no hash); `Digest = { entries }` (no\n273: high-water field); `DigestResult = { resend_from_seq: Option<i64>, pull_entities: Vec<Uuid> }`. 501\n274: implements the §A shapes EXACTLY and does not widen them — a hash/high-water field would be a Trap-6\n275: CONTRACT divergence requiring escalation first. **This still satisfies TS4:** the hive already knows its\n276: own cursor (`MAX(seq) FROM node_op_log WHERE node_id=$1`), so it does not need the node's high-water on\n277: the wire; and TS4's two divergences are **set-difference on `entity_id`** (via the\n278: `source_node_id + source_task_id` id bridge), not version comparisons. Recorded as a deliberate\n279: narrowing-to-contract, not an omission.\n280: \n281: ### Heal-on-EXISTENCE, not version equality (the noisy-version trap)\n282: `Task::update` bumps no local version (Phase-1 ledger judgment #3); `remote_version` is the hive's echoed\n283: value (0 pre-ack vs hive `version:1`), so version diffs are noisy for node-owned tasks and would thrash a\n284: version-gated heal. 503 drives `resend_from_seq`/`pull_entities` purely off entity EXISTENCE\n285: (set-difference on the id-bridge key), NOT version mismatch. `version` is carried in `DigestEntry` for\n286: future drift use but does not trigger heal in this tracer. STOP triggers in 503/504 enforce this.\n287: \n288: ### `resend_from_seq` requires a NEW `peek_from_seq` that IGNORES `acked_at` (504, +node_outbox.rs)\n289: A node-has/hive-lacks divergence means an **acked-but-lost** op (the hive applied then lost it, or the\n290: ack raced a crash). 107's `peek_unacked` filters `acked_at IS NULL` and therefore cannot reach such an\n291: op. 504 adds `OutboxRepository::peek_from_seq(pool, from_seq, limit)` (no `acked_at` predicate;\n292: `WHERE seq >= ?`) so acked rows replay. **Verified safe:** `mark_acked_through` only SETS `acked_at`\n293: (104), and `grep -rn \"DELETE.*node_outbox\"` finds NO prune of outbox rows anywhere — acked ops persist\n294: and are replayable. Over-resending is safe: 106's apply is idempotent (`ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`) and\n295: advances the ack only on a successful apply. This expands 504's `files:` to include\n296: `crates/db/src/models/node_outbox.rs`.\n297: \n298: ### Pull leg reuses the EXISTING bulk-snapshot reconcile (no per-entity pull)\n299: hive-has/node-lacks heals by re-running `sync_remote_projects` (node_runner.rs:941 — the reconcile\n300: gap-fill leg ADR-0008/ADR-0007 name), not a new per-entity fetch. `pull_entities` being non-empty is the\n301: TRIGGER to reconcile; the node lacks those local ids so it cannot look them up individually. The heal arm\n302: lives in `run_node_runner` (which holds `db.pool`, `remote_client`, and `handle.state.node_id()`/\n303: `organization_id()`), mirroring 108's `OpAck` seam (HiveClient is `&self`, holds no pool → emit a\n304: `HiveEvent::DigestResult`, do the work in the loop).\n305: \n306: ### \"On reconnect\" folded into \"first `sync_once` after reconnect\" (no distinct hook)\n307: There is no clean reconnect callback to anchor a digest send. The 30s `sync_once` loop (hive_sync.rs:131)\n308: is the only driver; a reconnect re-establishes the command channel and the next tick emits a fresh\n309: digest. 502 sends the digest at the tail of every `sync_once` (after 107's `sync_outbox`). No new\n310: reconnect hook was invented (would expand `files:` out of scope). Recorded so a reviewer expecting an\n311: explicit reconnect site understands the fold.\n312: \n313: ### TS4 acceptance lives in 503 (hive-side, fail-closed PG gate)\n314: 503 carries `covers_tests: [TS4]` and seeds the BIDIRECTIONAL divergence (node-has/hive-lacks +\n315: hive-has/node-lacks) inside a `#[cfg(test)] mod` in `session.rs` (the handler is private — same as 106).\n316: It REQUIRES a live migrated Postgres (incl. 102's `node_op_log`); the gate uses the\n317: `test -n \"$DATABASE_URL\" && …` fail-closed prefix (Trap 2b) so a skip is a hard fail, not a hollow green.\n318: The **\"no `reset_*` manual step\"** assertion is STRUCTURAL: convergence is produced purely by the\n319: returned `DigestResult` (consumed by 504 + the reconcile leg) with NO test-side SQL repair — that IS the\n320: SC5 contract. The hive compare also needs a new `SharedTaskRepository::list_source_task_versions_for_node`\n321: (filtering `deleted_at IS NULL` so a tombstoned task is not resurrected, ADR-0007 one-delete), expanding\n322: 503's `files:` to include `crates/remote/src/db/tasks.rs`.\n323: \n324: ### Cross-phase SHARED-FILE collision with P2's lease protocol (CONTRACT §A) — not yet wireable\n325: 501 hand-duplicates `Digest`/`DigestResult` into BOTH `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs` and\n326: `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs` (+ exhaustive arms in `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/session.rs`) —\n327: the SAME two enum files P2's lease-protocol task edits (`LeaseHeartbeat`/`LeaseGrant`/`LeaseRevoked`).\n328: CONTRACT §A: \"your protocol task SHARES message.rs+hive_client.rs with P2's lease protocol task.\" P2 is\n329: **not yet authored as task ids**, so 501's `conflicts_with` carries only the intra-P5 ids (503, 504) —\n330: `wai-plan-lint` enforces plan-table==frontmatter equality but does NOT require referenced ids to exist,\n331: so a forward reference to an unauthored P2 id would be a dangling-row risk. **Action for the P2 author:**\n332: when P2 lands, its protocol task MUST add 501 to its `conflicts_with`, 501 is updated symmetrically, and\n333: the two are `depends_on`-sequenced so they never edit the enum tails simultaneously (the dual-edit\n334: convention, Trap 3). Also note 601 (phase-6) already decision-locks `DigestResult@P5` in its exhaustive\n335: `HiveMessage` classification table — 501's variant is the one 601 expects.\n336: \n337: ### SHARED-FILE map across P5 (for cross-phase reviewers)\n338: - `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs` — 501 (variants), 504 (HiveEvent + arm). Also P1\n339:   103/108, P2 lease protocol.\n340: - `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs` — 501. Also P1 103, P2 lease protocol.\n341: - `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/session.rs` — 501 (stub arm), 503 (handler). Also P1 103/106.\n342: - `crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs` — 504. Also P1 108.\n343: - `crates/services/src/services/hive_sync.rs` — 502. Also P1 107.\n344: - `crates/db/src/models/node_outbox.rs` — 504. Also P1 104.\n345: - `crates/remote/src/db/tasks.rs`, `crates/db/src/models/task/queries.rs` — 503, 502 respectively\n346:   (new query methods beside existing ones).\n347: \n348: ### Lint note (expected-pending) — SC5/TS4 now CLAIMED by phase-5\n349: With phase-5 authored, `wai-plan-lint` SC5 moves unclaimed → claimed (502–504, `covers_criteria: [SC5]`)\n350: and TS4 → claimed (503, `covers_tests: [TS4]`). **501 carries `covers_criteria: []`** (not `[SC5]`) — it\n351: is a compile-only protocol-stub with an N/A failing test, and the lint rejects a non-empty\n352: `covers_criteria` paired with an N/A `## Failing test` (wai-plan-lint.sh:59-65); SC5 stays claimed by\n353: 502–504. This mirrors P1's 103 protocol-stub task exactly (`covers_criteria: []`, plan SC column\n354: informational). Remaining unclaimed ids are the still-unauthored phases\n355: (2,3,4,7 → SC3/SC4/SC7/SC6 + TS2/TS3/TS5/TS6) — the documented phase-by-phase state, not a failure.\n356: \n357: ## Phase-7 authoring — judgment calls (2026-06-30, NEEDS ORCHESTRATOR/USER RATIFICATION)\n358: \n359: Phase 7 (hive-only-state cutover, SC6/TS6 per ADR-0011) authored as 701/702/703. The most\n360: design-sensitive call (Trap 6) is surfaced for ratification.\n361: \n362: 1. **\"Rebuilt hive\" = IN-PLACE evolution, NOT a fresh-schema copy — RATIFICATION REQUESTED.** ADR-0011\n363:    says \"migrate … into the **rebuilt hive**.\" Two verified facts pin this to in-place: (a) no task in\n364:    this workstream rebuilds the hive schema — P1/P2 add only ADDITIVE migrations (`node_op_log` table,\n365:    `node_task_assignments` lease columns), nothing rebuilds `shared_tasks`; (b) the id bridge\n366:    (`source_task_id`/`source_node_id`) already exists as columns on `shared_tasks`\n367:    (`20260105120000_add_source_task_id.sql`) and is intact in place. The destructive alternative\n368:    (DROP+recreate `shared_tasks`, copy MUST-MIGRATE data across a fresh empty Postgres schema) would be\n369:    INVENTED and dangerous — NOT authored. **If the orchestrator/user wants a fresh-schema copy, 701/702/\n370:    703 must be re-authored** (each carries a STOP trigger for this).\n371: 2. **Cutover is a DATA operation (TRUNCATE/DELETE), NOT a schema DROP — load-bearing correction.** The\n372:    first draft of 701 DROPped the REGENERABLE/DISCARDABLE tables. Advisor + grep caught this: EVERY one\n373:    of those tables still has surviving `query!`/`query_as!` refs in `crates/remote/src` (`node_task_attempts`\n374:    13, `node_local_projects` 22, `activity` in `db/activity.rs`+`db/tasks.rs`, `auth_sessions` 8, …), and\n375:    NONE of that code is removed by THIS workstream (the removal lives in P4/P5, out of scope here). An\n376:    in-place `DROP TABLE` would (a) break `cargo check -p remote` online query validation, and (b) leave\n377:    no table for the node re-ingest path (`handle_attempt_sync` → `NodeTaskAttemptRepository::upsert`, an\n378:    `INSERT INTO`, NOT a `CREATE TABLE`) to repopulate. So 701 TRUNCATEs data and keeps schema.\n379: 2a. **701's test is seed→run-cutover-SQL→assert (non-hollow).** A naive \"connect + assert row_count==0\"\n380:    test would PASS on a fresh migrated PG even with an EMPTY migration body (nothing was ever inserted) —\n381:    the hollow-test class (tournament axis 7) reached via the migrate-on-empty-DB mechanism rather than\n382:    the skip guard. 701's test instead SEEDs rows (regenerable + discardable + must-migrate incl. an\n383:    ACTIVE and a COMPLETED assignment), re-runs the exact cutover statements (`CUTOVER_SQL`,\n384:    copy-identical to the migration body), then asserts cleared-vs-retained — catching a `TRUNCATE`\n385:    silently reaching a must-migrate table and an over-broad `DELETE` on active assignments. CASCADE/\n386:    RESTART IDENTITY are deliberately OMITTED (UUID PKs; a plain TRUNCATE that ERRORS on an external\n387:    inbound FK is the SAFE failure mode, not a silent must-migrate delete).\n388: 2b. **FROZEN-SPEC COLLISION — TS6 \"discardable tables are absent\" vs in-place keep-but-empty (NEEDS\n389:    RATIFICATION, Trap 6 / fidelity axis 9).** Spec TS6 literally says \"discardable tables are absent.\"\n390:    The in-place reading keeps them present-but-emptied (their `query!` refs are removed only in P4/P5,\n391:    and P7 depends on P1–P3 not P4/P5). Surfaced explicitly — NOT resolved by silently rewording 701's\n392:    assertion. Orchestrator/user must ratify (a) keep-but-empty satisfies TS6's \"nothing silently lost\"\n393:    intent (+ a spec note), OR (b) sequence a follow-up DROP migration AFTER the P4/P5 code-removal phase.\n394:    701 is authored for (a); 702 has no DISCARDABLE assertion; switching to (b) adds a later DROP task.\n395: 3. **Status enum needs NO remap of stored hive rows.** The hive `task_status` enum is ALREADY canonical\n396:    kebab-case `in-progress`/`in-review` (`20251001000000_shared_tasks_activity.sql:57`;\n397:    `crates/remote/src/db/tasks.rs:24`). The `inprogress`/`inreview`→kebab remap happens at the node→hive\n398:    INGEST boundary (op-log apply), so hive data-at-rest is already canonical. 702 therefore asserts the\n399:    value space is canonical (kebab accepted, node-lowercase rejected) + a round-trip preserves it, rather\n400:    than \"remapping\" existing rows.\n401: 4. **703 fidelity limitation (RATIFIED tracer-honesty).** The NEW ADR-0008 op-log re-ingest for\n402:    attempt/exec/log op types does NOT exist yet — P1 shipped only `task.upsert` (see \"Tracer honesty\"\n403:    above). So 703's \"simulated re-ingest\" drives the EXISTING `NodeTaskAttemptRepository::upsert` path\n404:    (what `handle_attempt_sync` uses today), proving the cutover leaves a refillable schema — NOT proving\n405:    the op-log mechanism. Stated in the test doc-comment.\n406: 5. **Already-removed tables NOT re-listed.** `node_projects` was dropped by `20260124200000`;\n407:    `project_activity_counters` was dropped then RECREATED in `20260124100000` (so it currently EXISTS and\n408:    IS cleared). The clear inventory was grounded against the live post-migration schema.\n409: 6. **Trap 2b (Postgres) applies to all three** — each states the live-PG precondition + the `test -n\n410:    \"$DATABASE_URL\" &&` fail-closed prefix. **701 is `irreversible: true`** (data loss) — gated behind\n411:    the ADR-0011 pre-cutover backup + a `reviews/701.approved` token.\n412: \n413: ### Lint note (expected-pending) — SC6/TS6 now CLAIMED by phase-7\n414: With phase-7 authored, `wai-plan-lint` SC6 moves unclaimed → claimed (701–703, `covers_criteria: [SC6]`)\n415: and TS6 → claimed (701–703, `covers_tests: [TS6]`). Remaining unclaimed ids are the still-unauthored\n416: phases (2,3,4 → SC3/SC4/SC7 + TS2/TS3/TS5) — the documented phase-by-phase state, not a failure.\n417: \n418: ### Phase-7 sibling-advisory acknowledgement (wai-plan-lint `W:` lines)\n419: - **701/702/703 tests beside `crates/remote/tests/backfill_e2e.rs`** — the genuine sibling. There is NO\n420:   shared `common` module in `remote/tests/`; each task READS `backfill_e2e.rs` and inlines its exact\n421:   `database_url()`/`skip_without_db!`/`create_pool()` helpers verbatim (same handling already ratified\n422:   for Phase-1 task 102). Acknowledged, handled in-task — not an unread reimplementation.\n423: - **701 migration beside `crates/remote/migrations/20251001000000_shared_tasks_activity.sql`** —\n424:   independent forward-only Postgres DDL/DML (the cutover data-clear), NOT a reimplementation of the init\n425:   schema. The real sibling for the data-clear shape is `20260124100000_remove_legacy_projects.sql` /\n426:   `20260124200000_remove_node_projects.sql` (named in 701's Change section), read for the\n427:   `DELETE FROM`/cleanup convention. Not a pattern sibling of the init migration.\n428: \n429: ## Phase-3 authoring — status state machine (SC4 / TS3) (2026-06-30)\n430: \n431: Phase-3 authored as 4 hive-only (`crates/remote`) tasks: 301 matrix module (new `status_machine.rs`),\n432: 302 canonical wire value, 303 enforcement at `handle_op_batch` (TS3), 304 legacy-path guard. **P3 adds NO\n433: WS variant** (CONTRACT §A: status rides the P1 op-log; Trap 3 does NOT apply). All four `covers_criteria\n434: [SC4]`; only 303 carries `covers_tests [TS3]`.\n435: \n436: ### ⚠️ OPEN ESCALATION (Trap 6 / CONTRACT-header \"record divergence HERE FIRST\") — ADR-0010 §D names enum values that do not exist\n437: **This BLOCKS execution of 301/303/304 and is recorded here per the CONTRACT header requirement before\n438: any code.** ADR-0010 §D and CONTRACT §D name node-reported `in-progress→failed` and hive-authored\n439: `todo→assigned`/`assigned→in-progress`/`assigned→todo`. **`Failed` and `Assigned` are NOT variants of\n440: `TaskStatus`** — both enums (node `crates/db/src/models/task/mod.rs:27`, hive `crates/remote/src/db/tasks.rs:25`)\n441: are exactly `Todo/InProgress/InReview/Done/Cancelled`. Conversely `InReview` exists in the enum and is\n442: PRODUCED by the live node path (`Completed→InReview`, `session.rs:672`) but is absent from §D's node list.\n443: So **§D is not encodable as written** — it references three non-existent values and omits one real one.\n444: 301 encodes a PROPOSED reconciliation (failures live in `execution_status`, not `task.status`; `assigned`\n445: collapses into `InProgress`; node terminals are `Done`+`InReview`; hive authors `Todo→InProgress` and\n446: `*→Cancelled`). This is a spec-vs-reality contradiction that **must be ratified by the user and recorded in\n447: CONTRACT §D before 301/303/304 execute** (Trap 6 — never paper over). Open questions surfaced to the user:\n448: 1. Does `task.status` have no `failed` (failures tracked at the execution/assignment level)?\n449: 2. Is the node terminal `Done`, `InReview`, or both — and is `InReview→Done` hive- or node-authored?\n450: 3. Is hive \"assigned\" simply `InProgress` (collapsing `todo→assigned→in-progress`)?\n451: 4. Is operator-unassign `InProgress→Todo` legal? (The proposed matrix currently makes it illegal — a\n452:    dropped §D row.)\n453: 5. Who authors `Running→InProgress` (a normal node \"running\" report on the legacy 304 path)? The proposed\n454:    matrix marks `Todo→InProgress` Hive-authored, which would REJECT a node \"running\" report on 304 — a\n455:    concrete symptom that dissolves once the matrix is ratified (do NOT patch 304 piecemeal first).\n456: Each of 301/303/304 carries a top-of-body `## ⚠️ OPEN ESCALATION` block pointing here; 301 owns the\n457: authoritative statement. **Once ratified, reconcile 301's matrix, 303's TS3 table, and 304's mapping, and\n458: update CONTRACT §D + ADR-0010 to the agreed values.**\n459: \n460: ### Judgment call — two status-write sites; BOTH gated (advisor §3), legacy path may be P4-retired\n461: The op-log path (106's `handle_op_batch` → `upsert_from_node`) is 303's site. A SECOND site writes\n462: `shared_tasks.status` from a node: the legacy `handle_task_status` (`session.rs:625`) →\n463: `update_status_from_node` (`tasks.rs:1009`), pure last-write-wins with no author/lease context (its\n464: `Failed|Cancelled→Todo` map at `session.rs:673` is exactly the clobber ADR-0010 removes). Gating ONLY the\n465: op-log path while claiming \"SC4 no field-level conflict closed\" would be a hole, so **304 routes the legacy\n466: write through the same `status_machine` guard**. 304's STOP triggers note that P4 (inbound-collapse) may\n467: instead DELETE the legacy path — if so 304 is superseded-obsolete (either outcome closes SC4's second\n468: site). Surfaced rather than silently single-gating.\n469: \n470: ### Judgment call — fencing is RIDDEN, not re-authored (CONTRACT §C / P2 seam)\n471: 303's \"node-reported transition accepted ONLY with valid lease+token\" rides P2's existing fencing check\n472: (CONTRACT §C: P2 adds the `op.fencing_token < assignment.fencing_token` reject to `handle_op_batch`). 303\n473: adds the ORTHOGONAL transition-legality guard (this from→to is node-authored) and gates on P2's lease+token\n474: decision; it does NOT re-implement the stale-token comparison. **P2's task id is unauthored**, so it is NOT\n475: in 303/304 `depends_on` — the P2 lease+fencing dependency is a prose PRECONDITION + STOP trigger (mirrors\n476: 106's Trap-2b precondition; sanctioned by the phase-by-phase model). If P2 has not landed\n477: (`node_task_assignments` lacks `fencing_token`/`lease_expires_at`, or `handle_op_batch` has no fencing\n478: seam), 303/304 STOP. **Raised: P3 cannot fully execute until P2 ships.**\n479: \n480: ### Judgment call — matrix in a NEW file (`status_machine.rs`), hermetic test; TS3 in 303 (Postgres, fail-closed)\n481: 301's matrix is a pure enum/fn → its unit test is hermetic (NO `DATABASE_URL`, no fail-closed prefix) so\n482: the author-legality table is never behind a DB skip. 302's canonicalization is likewise a hermetic\n483: `&str→TaskStatus` test. 303 (TS3 accept/reject with lease+fencing context) and 304 (legacy DB write) are\n484: Postgres-bound (Trap 2b) and use the FAIL-CLOSED `test -n \"$DATABASE_URL\" &&` gate prefix copied from 106.\n485: The fail-closed prefix is applied ONLY to the two Postgres-bound tasks. New file `status_machine.rs` is the\n486: only contention-free P3 artifact.\n487: \n488: ### SHARED FILE — `session.rs` (P1/106, P2, P3 all touch it)\n489: 302/303/304 all edit `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/session.rs`, the same file 106 (P1) and P2 (fencing) edit.\n490: 302↔303↔304 `conflicts_with` each other (session.rs); 301↔302 `conflicts_with` (both edit\n491: `status_machine.rs` — 301 creates, 302 extends). The P2 fencing edit to `handle_op_batch` and P3's status\n492: guard touch the SAME apply block — 303 explicitly names the seam (insert the author guard between 302's\n493: status-mapping and 106's `upsert_from_node`, gating on P2's lease/fencing decision) to avoid colliding with\n494: P2's edit. P2's task ids are unauthored so they cannot appear in P3 `conflicts_with` (same dangling-id\n495: constraint as the §C precondition) — recorded here.\n496: \n497: ### Lint note (expected-pending) — SC4/TS3 now CLAIMED by phase-3\n498: With phase-3 authored, `wai-plan-lint` SC4 + TS3 move unclaimed→claimed (301–304 `covers_criteria [SC4]`;\n499: 303 `covers_tests [TS3]`). The lint collects `covers_criteria`/`covers_tests` from EVERY phase task file\n500: with **no `status` filter** (`wai-plan-lint.sh:105` iterates all `phase-*/*.md`), so setting 301/303/304\n501: to `status: blocked` (matrix unratified — see escalation above) does NOT unclaim SC4/TS3; the coverage map\n502: stays satisfied while `/wai:next` correctly will NOT serve the blocked tasks. **plan.md task-table rows for\n503: phase-3 are NOT added by this AUTHOR-ONLY pass; they are an integration step** (the report carries the exact\n504: rows to paste, matching the final frontmatter).\n505: \n506: ### Lint FALSE POSITIVE — deferral-regex matches the `Todo` enum variant (cross-phase; analog of Trap 5)\n507: `wai-plan-lint` SC6 greps the `## Failing test` body `-qiE '(…|TODO|FIXME)'` (`wai-plan-lint.sh:64`,\n508: case-INSENSITIVE) to catch placeholder `TODO`/`FIXME` test stubs. The domain enum variant `TaskStatus::Todo`\n509: and the wire string `\"todo\"` — UNAVOIDABLE in a status-state-machine test — match `TODO` as a substring, so\n510: 301/302/303/304 are flagged \"Failing test defers\" **falsely**. Their tests are REAL (table-driven matrix\n511: assertions, not stubs). This is a tooling false positive on a legitimate enum name, the lint-side analog of\n512: Trap 5's precheck path-anchor truncation FP. **Phase-4's 403 hits the IDENTICAL `TaskStatus::Todo` FP**\n513: (confirmed) — it is cross-phase and pre-existing, not introduced here. Do NOT mangle valid Rust\n514: (`TaskStatus::Todo` is the real variant) to placate the regex. Resolution options for `/wai:close`: tighten\n515: the lint to word-boundary/uppercase-only `\\bTODO\\b|\\bFIXME\\b` (so it stops matching `Todo`), or accept the\n516: documented FP. Recorded so a lint re-run is not mistaken for a real \"deferred test\" defect.\n517: If `wai-plan-lint` enforces plan↔frontmatter row equality, those rows must be added at integration time.\n518: \n519: ## Phase-4 authoring — inbound collapse (SC7 / TS5, ADR-0007) (2026-06-30)\n520: \n521: Tasks 401–405. Five surgical tasks; all `covers_criteria [SC7]`; 401 is the consolidated TS5 acceptance\n522: (`covers_tests [TS5]`). Judgment calls surfaced (Trap 6) — ratify on integration:\n523: \n524: ### Judgment call — \"demote bulk snapshot to cold-start\" is VERIFY+GUARD, not a removal (RATIFIED in plan)\n525: The bulk-snapshot reconcile (`sync_remote_project_tasks` → `fetch_bulk_snapshot`) is invoked from EXACTLY\n526: ONE site — the `HiveEvent::Connected` arm of the node-runner loop (`node_runner.rs:677`). There is **no\n527: periodic task re-sync**: the only `tokio::time::sleep` in the file is the reconnect backoff\n528: (`node_runner.rs:1874`), and `spawn_hive_sync_service` (`:658`) syncs attempts/executions/logs, NOT\n529: tasks. So the snapshot is ALREADY cold-start/gap-fill, NOT a second continuous channel. ADR-0007's \"demote\n530: to reconcile-only\" is therefore met by construction; P4 makes it a **comment fence + topology STOP-trigger**\n531: (task 401), exactly mirroring the SC1 no-fanout \"largely already satisfied → verify + guard\" finding. A\n532: \"demote the snapshot\" task would have a no-op diff (hollow). **No spec edit** — SC7's \"collapsed to one\"\n533: is delivered by the delete/conflict/event-type fixes + the guard.\n534: \n535: ### Finding — LATENT PROD BUG: the WS leg's soft-unlink is a NO-OP for a linked row\n536: `process_task_deleted_event` (`processor.rs:437`) calls `set_shared_task_id(.., None)` by LOCAL id. That\n537: fn's WHERE is `id=$1 AND (shared_task_id IS NULL OR shared_task_id=$2) AND NOT EXISTS(…=$2…)`. With\n538: `$2 = NULL`: `shared_task_id = NULL` is never true (SQLite three-valued logic), so for a LINKED row\n539: (`shared_task_id = S`) the predicate is false → **0 rows updated → never unlinked**. Verified empirically\n540: (`UPDATE t SET s=NULL WHERE id=1 AND (s IS NULL OR s=NULL) …` leaves `s='S'`). So ADR-0007's premise \"the\n541: WS path soft-unlinks\" describes code that does NOT unlink a linked task. **Consequence:** task 402 routes\n542: BOTH legs through ONE working, executor-generic `unlink_by_shared_task_id` (`UPDATE … WHERE shared_task_id\n543: = ?`) — \"applied identically on both legs\" by construction (ADR-0007 §2). 402 therefore EXPANDS to touch\n544: `processor.rs` (not just `sync.rs` + `node_runner.rs`). This is a code-reality discovery achieving the\n545: spec's stated intent, so NO re-precheck — but it is a real latent bug worth calling out at integration.\n546: \n547: ### Judgment call — dirty-guard is ENTITY-LEVEL (skip whole apply), not field-level (RATIFIED)\n548: ADR-0007 §3 says \"never overwrites a field that has an unacked outbound op\". The node_outbox carries no\n549: per-field dirty tracking — only per-entity ops (`entity_id`). Task 403's guard is therefore entity-level:\n550: if `find_by_shared_task_id → local.id` has ANY unacked op (`acked_at IS NULL`), the WHOLE inbound apply is\n551: skipped. This is strictly MORE conservative than field-level (it overwrites nothing while dirty) and fully\n552: satisfies TS5's \"concurrent local edit not clobbered\". Placed INSIDE `upsert_remote_task` (the one fn both\n553: legs funnel through) so the guard is identical on both legs by construction. Field-level granularity would\n554: need a per-field dirty model the outbox doesn't carry — escalate if literal field-granularity is required.\n555: \n556: ### Judgment call — `task.reassigned` routes through the EXISTING upsert handler (RATIFIED)\n557: The hive emits `task.reassigned` with the IDENTICAL `SharedTaskActivityPayload { task, user }` as\n558: `task.updated` (`crates/remote/src/db/tasks.rs:982` → `insert_activity` builds the same payload; the new\n559: assignee is a field on `task`). Task 404 adds `\"task.reassigned\"` to the existing\n560: `\"task.created\" | \"task.updated\"` match arm — no separate handler (which would duplicate\n561: `process_task_upsert_event`).\n562: \n563: ### Electric removal (405) is CLEAN — verified, irreversible-flagged\n564: `ElectricTaskSyncService::sync_project_tasks` has ZERO runtime callers (grep: only doc-comments +\n565: `pub mod`). `extract_uuid_from_key` is used only by the file's own `#[cfg(test)]`. The SEPARATE\n566: `electric_sync` NDJSON client (mod.rs:7/57) STAYS — only `electric_task_sync` (the dead task-shape poll)\n567: is removed. The integration test `crates/services/tests/electric_task_sync.rs` imports `electric_sync`\n568: (the surviving client), NOT the deleted module — so it does not break. 405 is `irreversible: true`\n569: (whole-file delete) + `forbid_after: [electric_task_sync, ElectricTaskSyncService, sync_project_tasks]`;\n570: needs `reviews/405.approved`.\n571: \n572: ### SHARED-FILE map across P4 (for cross-phase reviewers)\n573: - `crates/db/src/models/task/sync.rs` — 402 (add `unlink_*` helpers), 403 (dirty-guard in\n574:   `upsert_remote_task`), 401 (TS5 test). 402↔403 `conflicts_with`; 401 sequenced after both via depends_on.\n575: - `crates/services/src/services/share/processor.rs` — 402 (WS-leg unlink repoint), 404 (reassigned arm).\n576:   402↔404 `conflicts_with`.\n577: - `crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs` — 402 (reconcile-leg repoint), 401 (comment fence).\n578:   Sequenced (401 depends_on 402).\n579: - `crates/db/src/models/node_outbox.rs` — 403 adds `has_unacked_for_entity` (cross-phase: P1 task 104\n580:   creates this file; 403 `depends_on: 104`).\n581: \n582: ### Lint note (expected-pending) — SC7/TS5 now CLAIMED by phase-4\n583: With phase-4 authored, `wai-plan-lint` SC7 + TS5 move unclaimed→claimed (401–405 `covers_criteria [SC7]`;\n584: 401 `covers_tests [TS5]`). plan.md phase-4 task-table rows ARE added by this pass (the inline edit) to\n585: keep plan↔frontmatter row-equality green. After phase-4, only SC1 (carved UI half) + the not-yet-authored\n586: phase-2 SC3/TS2 remain pending per the phase-by-phase plan.\n587: \n588: ## Phase-2 authoring — lease / atomic-checkout + fencing (SC3 / TS2, ADR-0009) (2026-06-30)\n589: \n590: Phase-2 authored as 10 tasks (201–210), all `covers_criteria: [SC3]`; 210 alone `covers_tests: [TS2]`.\n591: Anchors verified against current `main`. Judgment calls + reconciliations below (ratification welcome):\n592: \n593: 1. **`NodeTaskAssignment` FromRow column trap → narrow queries, struct NOT widened (203).** Adding\n594:    `lease_expires_at`/`fencing_token` to the `#[derive(FromRow)]` `NodeTaskAssignment` (domain.rs:155) would\n595:    break all ~9 existing `task_assignments.rs` SELECTs that omit them — sqlx `FromRow` `try_get`s every\n596:    field at RUNTIME (`ColumnNotFound`), `cargo check` stays green, the gate's tests go red. **Decision:**\n597:    201 adds the columns to the table only; 203/205/209 read them via narrow `RETURNING`/`query_scalar` into\n598:    a purpose `LeaseClaim` struct. The repo file uses **runtime** `sqlx::query_as::<_,T>`/`sqlx::query` (NOT\n599:    the `query!` macro), so the typecheck does not need the offline cache — only the tests need live PG. If a\n600:    later phase genuinely needs the columns on the struct, that is its own task editing all 9 column lists.\n601: \n602: 2. **Node fencing-token stamp is STREAM-TIME, not enqueue-time — prompt/contract divergence (207).** The\n603:    decompose prompt framed 207 as stamping at \"the outbox enqueue path.\" That is impossible-and-wrong-by-ADR:\n604:    the enqueue lives in `crates/db` (`task/queries.rs`, task 105), which has NO lease knowledge, and ADR-0009\n605:    §3 says the node stamps the token **it believes it holds at SEND time** (the stale token for a partitioned\n606:    node; `None` for node-owned work). The only place a node op is materialized onto the wire is `sync_outbox`\n607:    (P1/107, `hive_sync.rs`). **Decision:** 207 stamps there from the live lease; `node_outbox.fencing_token`\n608:    (col) stays NULL. This is a clean seam, NOT a user escalation.\n609: \n610: 3. **Lease state lives on `ActiveAssignment`, not a standalone `LeaseStore` (206/207/208 reconciled).** The\n611:    stamp (207) must look up the token BY `local_task_id`, but `LeaseGrant` carries only `assignment_id`. The\n612:    node already tracks `active_assignments: HashMap<assignment_id, ActiveAssignment{ …, local_task_id }>` on\n613:    the shared `Arc<RwLock<NodeRunnerState>>` (node_runner.rs:257). **Decision:** add `fencing_token:\n614:    Option<i64>` + `lease_expires_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>` as fields on `ActiveAssignment`; 206 writes them,\n615:    207 reads them (one map lookup), 208 reads `lease_expires_at` for the watchdog. One structure serves all\n616:    three — no extra Arc plumbing. 206 owns the field definitions; 207/208 only read (conflicts_with 206 on\n617:    node_runner.rs).\n618: \n619: 4. **`HiveSyncService.node_state` is `Option`, defaulting `None` (207 back-compat).** A required new ctor\n\n(Output capped at 50 KB.
