{"type":"tool_use","timestamp":1782856870942,"sessionID":"ses_0e57366b4ffeVAMRD3KZD8mtXC","part":{"type":"tool","tool":"bash","callID":"call_k00kaa3f","state":{"status":"completed","input":{"command":"for f in docs/plans/vk-swarm-hive-redesign/phase-2/*.md; do echo \"===== $f =====\"; cat \"$f\"; done","workdir":"/home/david/Code/vk-swarm/.claude/worktrees/bridge-cse_01B8B52jjMEdikaLRoA25qhr"},"output":"...output truncated...\n\nFull output saved to: /home/david/.local/share/opencode/tool-output/tool_f1a8cec08001TzSKSz0QnSUWgh\n\n  2. **Look up the active assignment by the shared id:**\n     `SELECT id, fencing_token FROM node_task_assignments WHERE task_id = $shared_id AND completed_at IS NULL`\n     (a narrow scalar/row read — do NOT use `NodeTaskAssignment` FromRow; the new column is not on that\n     struct — see 203's judgment call).\n  3. **No active assignment** → the fence does NOT apply (node-owned work or unassigned). Fall through to\n     106's normal apply. (`op.fencing_token` may be `None` here; that is correct — CONTRACT §C.)\n  4. **Active assignment present** → compare:\n     - If `op.fencing_token` is `None` OR `op.fencing_token < assignment.fencing_token` → **REJECT**: do\n       NOT call `upsert_from_node`, do NOT INSERT `node_op_log`, do NOT advance `applied_through_seq` past\n       this op. Emit `send_message(ws_sender, &HiveMessage::LeaseRevoked { assignment_id: <the assignment's\n       id from step 2>, reason: \"stale fencing token\".into() })` — the partitioned writer learns its lease\n       is gone. Then STOP applying this op (the contract says do NOT advance high-water past a rejected op;\n       mirror 106's PARK control-flow of NOT advancing, but this is a permanent reject, not a transient\n       park — log at warn, and break/return so the cursor does not skip it). Record the precise control\n       choice (break vs continue-without-advance) in the ledger; the test asserts the high-water does not\n       pass the rejected seq.\n     - If `op.fencing_token >= assignment.fencing_token` → the rightful current holder: fall through to\n       106's normal apply.\n  > **Scope (ADR-0009 §3):** the fence applies ONLY to ops against a hive-assigned task. Node-owned work\n  > (no assignment) carries `fencing_token = None` and is committed under the node's ownership identity —\n  > the stale-token check MUST NOT bounce it. The third test guards this.\n- **ws-free split:** if 106 extracted a `handle_op_batch_apply` (no `ws_sender`) for testability, the\n  fencing REJECT must still surface the `LeaseRevoked` emission. Either (a) thread an \"ops to revoke\"\n  `Vec<(assignment_id, reason)>` out of the apply fn and have `handle_op_batch` send them after, or (b)\n  keep the send in the wire fn. Pick one, mirror 106's split, and record it.\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY: add the active-assignment lookup + the stale-token guard inside `handle_op_batch`'s apply path, the\n`LeaseRevoked` emission on reject, and the fencing test(s). Reuse the existing context resolution from 106,\n`send_message`, and `HiveMessage::LeaseRevoked` (202). Do NOT re-implement 106's apply/park/skip logic, do\nNOT touch `try_claim`/`renew_lease` (203), the WS enums (202), `handle_lease_heartbeat` (204), the node\nside, or any migration.\n\n## STOP triggers\n- The fence bounces an op whose task has NO active assignment (node-owned work, `fencing_token = None`) →\n  BUG: the fence is scoped to hive-assigned tasks (CONTRACT §C). Only ops whose task has an active\n  assignment are subject to the token compare. The third test catches this.\n- A rejected op ADVANCES `applied_through_seq` (or records a `node_op_log` dedup row) → BUG: a stale op must\n  NOT be acked; advancing past it would let the node believe a bounced write was committed (silent loss in\n  reverse). Do NOT advance, do NOT record. The first test asserts the high-water is unchanged.\n- Keying the assignment lookup on the SENDER's `node_id`/`local_task_id` instead of the resolved\n  `shared_tasks.id` → **THE SC3-BREAKING BUG**: after reassignment the active row is node B's, so a\n  sender-keyed lookup finds nothing, the stale op falls through and APPLIES = double execution. The fence\n  MUST resolve `find_by_source_task_id(node_id, payload.id) → shared id` first, then look up the assignment\n  by that shared id. The first test seeds the full reassignment so a wrong key makes it fail (non-hollow).\n- Comparing against the WRONG token (e.g. the node's claimed token instead of the assignment's CURRENT\n  token) → BUG: the authority is `node_task_assignments.fencing_token` (bumped on every (re)claim by 201's\n  sequence). Read it live per op.\n- `handle_op_batch` (106) is absent or its loop shape differs from the read → STOP: 205 depends on 106\n  having landed (depends_on: 106). If 106 drifted, re-locate the apply branch and record.\n- Using `NodeTaskAssignment` FromRow to read `fencing_token` → STOP: the column is NOT on that struct\n  (203's judgment call). Use a narrow `SELECT fencing_token, id` scalar/row read.\n\n## Done when\n`WAI_TYPECHECK_CMD=\"cargo check -p remote\" WAI_TEST_CMD='test -n \"$DATABASE_URL\" && cargo test -p remote fencing' bash ~/.claude/wai/scripts/task-gate.sh vk-swarm-hive-redesign 205` exits 0\n(run with `DATABASE_URL=postgres://…` against a migrated Postgres — Trap 2b; `test -n` prefix FAIL-CLOSED.\nIf the tests live in the `op_batch_tests` module instead of a `fencing` module, set the test filter to the\nmodule/test names you used and record it.)\n===== docs/plans/vk-swarm-hive-redesign/phase-2/206-node-lease-state.md =====\n---\nid: \"206\"\nphase: 2\ntitle: Node lease state — HiveEvent Lease variants, store token+expiry on ActiveAssignment, send LeaseHeartbeat\nstatus: ready\ndepends_on: [\"202\"]\nparallel: false\nconflicts_with: [\"202\", \"207\", \"208\"]\nfiles:\n  - crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs\n  - crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs\nirreversible: false\nscope_test: \"crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs\"\nallowed_change: edit\ncovers_criteria: [SC3]\ncovers_tests: []\n---\n## Failing test (write first)\nA live round-trip is out of hermetic scope here (the WS connection + hive are integration concerns\ncovered by 210); this task's own obligation is the node-local lease **store** + the `HiveEvent` plumbing.\nAdd a hermetic unit test (no\nDB, no WS — the state is in-memory) in a `#[cfg(test)] mod` inside `node_runner.rs` beside the existing\ntests. The lease fields live ON `ActiveAssignment` in `NodeRunnerState` (NOT a separate store — see Change),\nso the test exercises the grant/revoke effect on that map:\n```rust\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod lease_state_tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn lease_grant_sets_token_and_expiry_on_active_assignment_then_revoke_clears() {\n        let state = std::sync::Arc::new(tokio::sync::RwLock::new(NodeRunnerState::default()));\n        let aid = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        let local = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        // Seed an active assignment (as HiveEvent::TaskAssigned would).\n        state.write().await.active_assignments.insert(aid, ActiveAssignment {\n            assignment_id: aid, task_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4(), local_task_id: Some(local),\n            local_attempt_id: None, status: TaskExecutionStatus::Pending,\n            fencing_token: None, lease_expires_at: None,\n        });\n        let expires = chrono::Utc::now() + chrono::Duration::seconds(60);\n\n        // apply_lease_grant is the small helper the process_event arm calls (testable, no WS).\n        apply_lease_grant(&state, aid, 7, expires).await;\n        {\n            let s = state.read().await;\n            let a = s.active_assignments.get(&aid).unwrap();\n            assert_eq!(a.fencing_token, Some(7));\n            assert_eq!(a.lease_expires_at, Some(expires));\n        }\n        // A higher token replaces a lower one; a grant never lowers a token.\n        apply_lease_grant(&state, aid, 9, expires).await;\n        assert_eq!(state.read().await.active_assignments.get(&aid).unwrap().fencing_token, Some(9));\n\n        apply_lease_revoke(&state, aid).await;\n        assert_eq!(state.read().await.active_assignments.get(&aid).unwrap().fencing_token, None);\n    }\n}\n```\n> Match `TaskExecutionStatus`'s real variant name (read it; the literal above is illustrative). If you\n> prefer inline arms over `apply_lease_grant`/`apply_lease_revoke` helpers, test the equivalent effect;\n> keep the test ws-free and db-free. Record the placement in the ledger.\n\n## Change\nThis is the **consumer** task for the 202 wire variants — it mirrors Phase-1 task 108 (which added\n`HiveEvent::OpAck` + the node_runner arm for the 103 stub). `HiveEvent`'s ONLY two sites are\n`hive_client.rs` (definition + `handle_hive_message` emit) and `node_runner.rs` (`process_event` consume) —\ngrep-verified in the Phase-1 ledger (#5). No third match site.\n\n**DESIGN (reconciled with 207/208 — decisions-ledger judgment call):** the per-task fencing token must be\nlooked up at op-stream time BY `local_task_id` (207) and the lease expiry read for the watchdog (208). The\nnode already tracks `active_assignments: HashMap<assignment_id, ActiveAssignment{ …, local_task_id }>` on\nthe shared `Arc<RwLock<NodeRunnerState>>` (node_runner.rs:257, populated @423). So the lease state lives as\n**two new fields on `ActiveAssignment`**, NOT a separate `LeaseStore` — one structure serves 206/207/208 and\nkeeps the `local_task_id → token` lookup a single map read.\n\n### 1. `crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs`\n- **Anchor A — `struct ActiveAssignment` (@238-246):** add two fields:\n```rust\n    /// Current fencing token from the hive lease grant (SC3). None until a LeaseGrant arrives, or for\n    /// node-owned work (no hive assignment).\n    pub fencing_token: Option<i64>,\n    /// Lease expiry from the hive (SC3). The self-fence watchdog (task 208) halts the agent if this\n    /// passes without a renewal.\n    pub lease_expires_at: Option<chrono::DateTime<Utc>>,\n```\n  Update the `ActiveAssignment { … }` literal where assignments are inserted (@423-428) to set both to\n  `None` initially (the grant fills them). (`Utc` is in scope — the file uses `chrono`/`Utc` already; if\n  not imported, add `use chrono::{DateTime, Utc};` confined to this file.)\n- **Anchor B — `process_event` match (@341, exhaustive over `&HiveEvent`):** add arms for the two new\n  variants (added in step 2), mirroring the existing `TaskAssigned`/`TaskCancelled` arms that already\n  `self.state.write().await` and mutate `active_assignments`:\n```rust\n            HiveEvent::LeaseGranted { assignment_id, fencing_token, lease_expires_at } => {\n                apply_lease_grant(&self.state, *assignment_id, *fencing_token, *lease_expires_at).await;\n                tracing::debug!(%assignment_id, fencing_token, \"stored lease grant\");\n            }\n            HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked { assignment_id, reason } => {\n                apply_lease_revoke(&self.state, *assignment_id).await;\n                tracing::warn!(%assignment_id, %reason, \"lease revoked — agent halt is task 208\");\n                // The actual agent halt is task 208's watchdog/handler; here we only clear the lease.\n            }\n```\n  Add the two small free helpers (testable, ws-free) near the bottom of the module:\n```rust\n    async fn apply_lease_grant(\n        state: &std::sync::Arc<tokio::sync::RwLock<NodeRunnerState>>,\n        assignment_id: Uuid, fencing_token: i64, lease_expires_at: chrono::DateTime<Utc>,\n    ) {\n        let mut s = state.write().await;\n        if let Some(a) = s.active_assignments.get_mut(&assignment_id) {\n            // Never lower a token (monotonic): only accept a >= token.\n            if a.fencing_token.map_or(true, |t| fencing_token >= t) {\n                a.fencing_token = Some(fencing_token);\n                a.lease_expires_at = Some(lease_expires_at);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    async fn apply_lease_revoke(\n        state: &std::sync::Arc<tokio::sync::RwLock<NodeRunnerState>>, assignment_id: Uuid,\n    ) {\n        let mut s = state.write().await;\n        if let Some(a) = s.active_assignments.get_mut(&assignment_id) {\n            a.fencing_token = None;\n            a.lease_expires_at = None;\n        }\n    }\n```\n- **Anchor C — periodic `LeaseHeartbeat` sender:** where the runner spawns its background tasks (near @658,\n  the `spawn_hive_sync_service` / `command_tx` clone), spawn a task that on an interval STRICTLY SHORTER\n  than the hive `LEASE_TTL` (204) sends `command_tx.send(NodeMessage::LeaseHeartbeat { assignment_ids })`\n  where `assignment_ids` = the keys of `state.read().await.active_assignments`. Use the existing\n  `tokio::time::interval` pattern (see hive_sync.rs:131). The filter `sync_outbox` runs both 107's and 207's tests in that module.)\n===== docs/plans/vk-swarm-hive-redesign/phase-2/208-node-self-fence-watchdog.md =====\n---\nid: \"208\"\nphase: 2\ntitle: Node self-fence watchdog — halt the agent on lease-revoke or renew-deadline miss\nstatus: ready\ndepends_on: [\"206\"]\nparallel: false\nconflicts_with: [\"206\", \"207\"]\nfiles:\n  - crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs\nirreversible: false\nscope_test: \"crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs\"\nallowed_change: edit\ncovers_criteria: [SC3]\ncovers_tests: []\n---\n## Failing test (write first)\nHermetic, ws-free, db-free unit test of the **decision** the watchdog makes — \"which assignments are past\ntheir renew deadline / revoked and must be fenced\" — separated from the actual `stop_execution` side\neffect (which needs a container + DB). In `node_runner.rs`'s `#[cfg(test)] mod` (beside 206's\n`lease_state_tests`):\n```rust\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod self_fence_tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn assignments_with_expired_or_missing_lease_are_selected_for_fencing() {\n        let state = std::sync::Arc::new(tokio::sync::RwLock::new(NodeRunnerState::default()));\n        let live = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        let expired = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        let revoked = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        {\n            let mut s = state.write().await;\n            let mk = |aid, expires| ActiveAssignment {\n                assignment_id: aid, task_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4(), local_task_id: Some(uuid::Uuid::new_v4()),\n                local_attempt_id: Some(uuid::Uuid::new_v4()), status: TaskExecutionStatus::Running,\n                fencing_token: Some(1), lease_expires_at: expires,\n            };\n            // live: lease in the future → NOT fenced.\n            s.active_assignments.insert(live, mk(live, Some(chrono::Utc::now() + chrono::Duration::seconds(60))));\n            // expired: lease in the past → fenced (renew-deadline miss).\n            s.active_assignments.insert(expired, mk(expired, Some(chrono::Utc::now() - chrono::Duration::seconds(1))));\n            // revoked: lease cleared by HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked (token+expiry None) but still Running → fenced.\n            let mut r = mk(revoked, None); r.fencing_token = None;\n            s.active_assignments.insert(revoked, r);\n        }\n        let to_fence = assignments_to_self_fence(&state, chrono::Utc::now()).await;\n        assert!(to_fence.contains(&expired), \"an expired lease self-fences (ADR-0009)\");\n        assert!(to_fence.contains(&revoked), \"a revoked lease self-fences\");\n        assert!(!to_fence.contains(&live), \"a live lease is not fenced\");\n    }\n}\n```\n> Match `TaskExecutionStatus`'s real variant names (read them). The pure selector\n> `assignments_to_self_fence(&state, now) -> Vec<Uuid>` is testable without a container; the watchdog loop\n> calls it then invokes the halt path on each id. Record this split in the ledger.\n\n## Change\nThis reuses the EXISTING agent-halt mechanism (ADR-0001 / ADR-0009 §4): `AssignmentHandler::handle_cancellation`\n(`assignment_handler.rs:194`) already finds the assignment's running execution processes and calls\n`container.stop_execution(.., Killed)` — the process-group kill. The self-fence is a watchdog that invokes\nthat SAME halt when a lease cannot be renewed within its TTL (or is revoked). It does NOT re-implement the kill.\n\n- **File:** `crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs`\n- **Anchor A — the pure selector** (new free fn near 206's `apply_lease_*` helpers):\n```rust\n    /// Assignments whose hive lease has lapsed (expired or revoked) while still Running — the node must\n    /// self-fence their agents (ADR-0009 §4: bounded overlap). A revoked lease has `lease_expires_at = None`\n    /// (cleared by HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked, task 206) but a still-Running status; an expired lease has\n    /// `lease_expires_at < now`. A live lease (future expiry) is left alone.\n    async fn assignments_to_self_fence(\n        state: &std::sync::Arc<tokio::sync::RwLock<NodeRunnerState>>,\n        now: chrono::DateTime<Utc>,\n    ) -> Vec<Uuid> {\n        let s = state.read().await;\n        s.active_assignments.values()\n            .filter(|a| matches!(a.status, TaskExecutionStatus::Running)) // only halt live execution\n            .filter(|a| match a.lease_expires_at {\n                Some(exp) => exp < now,   // renew-deadline miss\n                None => a.fencing_token.is_none(), // revoked (lease cleared) — distinguishes from\n                                                   // never-yet-granted? see STOP triggers\n            })\n            .map(|a| a.assignment_id)\n            .collect()\n    }\n```\n  > **Never-granted vs revoked ambiguity (STOP trigger below):** a freshly-assigned assignment that has not\n  > YET received its first `LeaseGrant` also has `lease_expires_at = None`. Do NOT fence it (it is starting,\n  > not lapsed). The watchdog MUST only consider assignments that were once granted then lost their lease.\n  > Resolve by gating the `None` arm on a \"was previously leased\" signal — e.g. add a `lease_revoked: bool`\n  > flag set by 206's `apply_lease_revoke`, OR only fence on `Some(exp) where exp < now` (expiry) and let\n  > the explicit `HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked` arm (206) trigger an immediate fence directly (preferred — see\n  > Anchor C). Pick ONE and record it; the simplest is: watchdog fences on EXPIRY only, and the\n  > `LeaseRevoked` event arm fences immediately. Then the `None`/`fencing_token.is_none()` leg above is\n  > unnecessary — drop it and fence only `Some(exp) < now`.\n- **Anchor B — the watchdog loop:** where the runner spawns background tasks (near @658, beside 206's\n  `LeaseHeartbeat` sender), spawn a `tokio::time::interval` loop (cadence ≤ the lease TTL granularity, e.g.\n  every few seconds) that calls `assignments_to_self_fence(&state, Utc::now())` and, for each id, invokes\n  the halt. The halt needs the `AssignmentHandler` (which owns `container` + `db`). The handler is built at\n  @662-663 (`Option<AssignmentHandler<C>>`); clone what `handle_cancellation` needs, OR call\n  `handler.handle_cancellation(assignment_id)` directly (it sets status to `Cancelled` and stops processes —\n  acceptable as the fence effect; a dedicated `self_fence(assignment_id)` that sets a Failed/Fenced status\n  is nicer but reuses the same stop logic). Reuse `handle_cancellation` unless a distinct status is required;\n  record the choice.\n- **Anchor C — immediate fence on revoke:** in 206's `HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked` arm (which 206 added to\n  `process_event`), ADD the immediate halt: after clearing the lease, invoke the same halt path for that\n  assignment id (the partitioned node learns its lease is gone and stops NOW, not at the next watchdog tick).\n  This is the one line 208 adds to the 206-authored arm (hence conflicts_with: 206 on this file).\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY: add `assignments_to_self_fence`, spawn the watchdog loop, invoke the existing halt\n(`AssignmentHandler::handle_cancellation` or a thin `self_fence` wrapper around the same stop logic) on\nselected/revoked assignments, and the immediate-fence line in the `LeaseRevoked` arm, plus the\n`self_fence_tests` module. TS2\n(spec `## Test strategy`): *\"Lease a task to node A; simulate A partitioned but alive; expire + reassign to\nB (higher fencing token); assert A's late commit is **rejected by stale-token** and A **self-fences** (agent\nhalted) within TTL — at-most-once effect, bounded overlap.\"*\n\n**PRECONDITION (Trap 2b — NON-NEGOTIABLE):** the stale-token-reject half exercises the hive op-apply +\nfencing against a live, migrated Postgres. TS2 (SC3): a partition cannot cause double execution — stale-token commit is rejected.\nuse sqlx::PgPool;\nuse remote::db::task_assignments::TaskAssignmentRepository;\n\nfn database_url() -> Option<String> { std::env::var(\"DATABASE_URL\").ok() }\nmacro_rules! skip_without_db { () => {\n    if database_url().is_none() { eprintln!(\"Skipping: DATABASE_URL not set\"); return; }\n}; }\nasync fn create_pool() -> PgPool { PgPool::connect(&database_url().unwrap()).await.expect(\"connect\") }\n// … inline create_test_organization / create_test_node + seed (task_id, node_project_id).\n\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn partitioned_node_late_commit_is_rejected_after_reassignment() {\n    skip_without_db!();\n    let pool = create_pool().await;\n    let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n    // 1. Lease task T to node A (token T1). Use an already-past TTL to simulate the partition window.\n    let a = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(-1))\n        .await.unwrap().expect(\"A wins\");\n    // 2. A is partitioned-but-alive. The lease-expiry SWEEP (209) reclaims the expired lease, bumping the\n    //    token (exercises reclaim_expired_leases — why 210 depends_on 209). Then reassign to node B.\n    let reclaimed = repo.reclaim_expired_leases().await.unwrap();\n    assert!(reclaimed.iter().any(|r| r.task_id == task_id), \"the sweep reclaimed A's expired lease\");\n    let b = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_b, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n        .await.unwrap().expect(\"B claims the reclaimed task\");\n    assert!(b.fencing_token > a.fencing_token, \"B's token is strictly higher (partition-safety basis)\");\n    // 3. A's late commit (stamped with the OLD token T1) is STALE vs the assignment's current token T2.\n    //    Drive it through the seam 205 exposes (see scope note) and assert:\n    //      - the shared_task is NOT updated by A's stale op,\n    //      - the assignment's current fencing_token is STILL T2 (A's op did not roll it back),\n    //      - the rejection is surfaced (LeaseRevoked for A / an error) — A learns its lease is gone.\n    //    => at-most-once COMMIT effect: only the rightful holder (B, token T2) can commit.\n    let _ = (a, b);\n}\n```\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY create the one `tests/lease_partition_e2e.rs` integration test. The filter `sync_outbox` runs both 107's and 207's tests in that module.)\n===== docs/plans/vk-swarm-hive-redesign/phase-2/208-node-self-fence-watchdog.md =====\n---\nid: \"208\"\nphase: 2\ntitle: Node self-fence watchdog — halt the agent on lease-revoke or renew-deadline miss\nstatus: ready\ndepends_on: [\"206\"]\nparallel: false\nconflicts_with: [\"206\", \"207\"]\nfiles:\n  - crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs\nirreversible: false\nscope_test: \"crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs\"\nallowed_change: edit\ncovers_criteria: [SC3]\ncovers_tests: []\n---\n## Failing test (write first)\nHermetic, ws-free, db-free unit test of the **decision** the watchdog makes — \"which assignments are past\ntheir renew deadline / revoked and must be fenced\" — separated from the actual `stop_execution` side\neffect (which needs a container + DB). In `node_runner.rs`'s `#[cfg(test)] mod` (beside 206's\n`lease_state_tests`):\n```rust\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod self_fence_tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn assignments_with_expired_or_missing_lease_are_selected_for_fencing() {\n        let state = std::sync::Arc::new(tokio::sync::RwLock::new(NodeRunnerState::default()));\n        let live = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        let expired = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        let revoked = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        {\n            let mut s = state.write().await;\n            let mk = |aid, expires| ActiveAssignment {\n                assignment_id: aid, task_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4(), local_task_id: Some(uuid::Uuid::new_v4()),\n                local_attempt_id: Some(uuid::Uuid::new_v4()), status: TaskExecutionStatus::Running,\n                fencing_token: Some(1), lease_expires_at: expires,\n            };\n            // live: lease in the future → NOT fenced.\n            s.active_assignments.insert(live, mk(live, Some(chrono::Utc::now() + chrono::Duration::seconds(60))));\n            // expired: lease in the past → fenced (renew-deadline miss).\n            s.active_assignments.insert(expired, mk(expired, Some(chrono::Utc::now() - chrono::Duration::seconds(1))));\n            // revoked: lease cleared by HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked (token+expiry None) but still Running → fenced.\n            let mut r = mk(revoked, None); r.fencing_token = None;\n            s.active_assignments.insert(revoked, r);\n        }\n        let to_fence = assignments_to_self_fence(&state, chrono::Utc::now()).await;\n        assert!(to_fence.contains(&expired), \"an expired lease self-fences (ADR-0009)\");\n        assert!(to_fence.contains(&revoked), \"a revoked lease self-fences\");\n        assert!(!to_fence.contains(&live), \"a live lease is not fenced\");\n    }\n}\n```\n> Match `TaskExecutionStatus`'s real variant names (read them). The pure selector\n> `assignments_to_self_fence(&state, now) -> Vec<Uuid>` is testable without a container; the watchdog loop\n> calls it then invokes the halt path on each id. Record this split in the ledger.\n\n## Change\nThis reuses the EXISTING agent-halt mechanism (ADR-0001 / ADR-0009 §4): `AssignmentHandler::handle_cancellation`\n(`assignment_handler.rs:194`) already finds the assignment's running execution processes and calls\n`container.stop_execution(.., Killed)` — the process-group kill. The self-fence is a watchdog that invokes\nthat SAME halt when a lease cannot be renewed within its TTL (or is revoked). It does NOT re-implement the kill.\n\n- **File:** `crates/services/src/services/node_runner.rs`\n- **Anchor A — the pure selector** (new free fn near 206's `apply_lease_*` helpers):\n```rust\n    /// Assignments whose hive lease has lapsed (expired or revoked) while still Running — the node must\n    /// self-fence their agents (ADR-0009 §4: bounded overlap). A revoked lease has `lease_expires_at = None`\n    /// (cleared by HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked, task 206) but a still-Running status; an expired lease has\n    /// `lease_expires_at < now`. A live lease (future expiry) is left alone.\n    async fn assignments_to_self_fence(\n        state: &std::sync::Arc<tokio::sync::RwLock<NodeRunnerState>>,\n        now: chrono::DateTime<Utc>,\n    ) -> Vec<Uuid> {\n        let s = state.read().await;\n        s.active_assignments.values()\n            .filter(|a| matches!(a.status, TaskExecutionStatus::Running)) // only halt live execution\n            .filter(|a| match a.lease_expires_at {\n                Some(exp) => exp < now,   // renew-deadline miss\n                None => a.fencing_token.is_none(), // revoked (lease cleared) — distinguishes from\n                                                   // never-yet-granted? see STOP triggers\n            })\n            .map(|a| a.assignment_id)\n            .collect()\n    }\n```\n  > **Never-granted vs revoked ambiguity (STOP trigger below):** a freshly-assigned assignment that has not\n  > YET received its first `LeaseGrant` also has `lease_expires_at = None`. Do NOT fence it (it is starting,\n  > not lapsed). The watchdog MUST only consider assignments that were once granted then lost their lease.\n  > Resolve by gating the `None` arm on a \"was previously leased\" signal — e.g. add a `lease_revoked: bool`\n  > flag set by 206's `apply_lease_revoke`, OR only fence on `Some(exp) where exp < now` (expiry) and let\n  > the explicit `HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked` arm (206) trigger an immediate fence directly (preferred — see\n  > Anchor C). Pick ONE and record it; the simplest is: watchdog fences on EXPIRY only, and the\n  > `LeaseRevoked` event arm fences immediately. Then the `None`/`fencing_token.is_none()` leg above is\n  > unnecessary — drop it and fence only `Some(exp) < now`.\n- **Anchor B — the watchdog loop:** where the runner spawns background tasks (near @658, beside 206's\n  `LeaseHeartbeat` sender), spawn a `tokio::time::interval` loop (cadence ≤ the lease TTL granularity, e.g.\n  every few seconds) that calls `assignments_to_self_fence(&state, Utc::now())` and, for each id, invokes\n  the halt. The halt needs the `AssignmentHandler` (which owns `container` + `db`). The handler is built at\n  @662-663 (`Option<AssignmentHandler<C>>`); clone what `handle_cancellation` needs, OR call\n  `handler.handle_cancellation(assignment_id)` directly (it sets status to `Cancelled` and stops processes —\n  acceptable as the fence effect; a dedicated `self_fence(assignment_id)` that sets a Failed/Fenced status\n  is nicer but reuses the same stop logic). Reuse `handle_cancellation` unless a distinct status is required;\n  record the choice.\n- **Anchor C — immediate fence on revoke:** in 206's `HiveEvent::LeaseRevoked` arm (which 206 added to\n  `process_event`), ADD the immediate halt: after clearing the lease, invoke the same halt path for that\n  assignment id (the partitioned node learns its lease is gone and stops NOW, not at the next watchdog tick).\n  This is the one line 208 adds to the 206-authored arm (hence conflicts_with: 206 on this file).\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY: add `assignments_to_self_fence`, spawn the watchdog loop, invoke the existing halt\n(`AssignmentHandler::handle_cancellation` or a thin `self_fence` wrapper around the same stop logic) on\nselected/revoked assignments, and the immediate-fence line in the `LeaseRevoked` arm, plus the\n`self_fence_tests` module. / create_pool + org/node fixtures (as 203).\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn reclaim_expired_leases_bumps_token_and_returns_reclaimed_assignments() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        // node_a claims a task with an ALREADY-PAST TTL (lease_expires_at < now).\n        let a = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(-1))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        // Sweep reclaims expired leases.\n        let reclaimed = repo.reclaim_expired_leases().await.unwrap();\n        assert!(reclaimed.iter().any(|r| r.assignment_id == a.assignment_id),\n            \"an expired lease is reclaimed by the sweep\");\n        let r = reclaimed.iter().find(|r| r.assignment_id == a.assignment_id).unwrap();\n        assert!(r.fencing_token > a.fencing_token,\n            \"reclaim bumps the fencing token strictly higher (so the old holder's late ops are stale)\");\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn sweep_does_not_touch_live_leases() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        let _live = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        let reclaimed = repo.reclaim_expired_leases().await.unwrap();\n        assert!(reclaimed.iter().all(|r| r.task_id != task_id), \"a live lease is not reclaimed\");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Change\n### 1. `crates/remote/src/db/task_assignments.rs` — the reclaim query\n- **Anchor:** add `reclaim_expired_leases` inside `impl<'a> TaskAssignmentRepository<'a>`, beside\n  `fail_node_assignments` (@329-349, the existing `UPDATE … WHERE completed_at IS NULL RETURNING` read with\n  `.get(...)` — the exact pattern to mirror). TS2\n(spec `## Test strategy`): *\"Lease a task to node A; simulate A partitioned but alive; expire + reassign to\nB (higher fencing token); assert A's late commit is **rejected by stale-token** and A **self-fences** (agent\nhalted) within TTL — at-most-once effect, bounded overlap.\"*\n\n**PRECONDITION (Trap 2b — NON-NEGOTIABLE):** the stale-token-reject half exercises the hive op-apply +\nfencing against a live, migrated Postgres. TS2 is proven as TWO coordinated assertions over the\nreal units, NOT a mocked end-to-end:\n1. **Hive stale-token rejection (the at-most-once commit effect)** — an integration test here in\n   `crates/remote/tests/` that drives the real `try_claim` (203) → reclaim-with-higher-token (209's sweep\n   query or a second `try_claim` after expiry) → then applies a node-A op stamped with the OLD token and\n   asserts the hive REJECTS it (no apply, no advance, `LeaseRevoked` surfaced) per 205. This is the\n   commit-effect guarantee.\n2. **Node self-fence (bounded overlap)** — covered by 208's hermetic `self_fence_tests`\n   (`assignments_to_self_fence` selects an expired/revoked Running assignment for halt) + 206's lease-state\n   test. This task ASSERTS that coverage exists by reference (it cannot import the node `services` test\n   module from the `remote` crate); the ledger records the two test names as the self-fence evidence.\n\n> Because 205's fencing check is PRIVATE to `session.rs`, this `tests/` integration test cannot call\n> `handle_op_batch` directly. Drive the rejection through the SAME seam 205's own `#[cfg(test)] mod` uses —\n> i.e. if 205 extracted a `pub(crate)`-or-test-visible apply entry, reuse it; otherwise this acceptance\n> test asserts the rejection at the REPOSITORY layer it CAN reach: a stale-token op's effect is \"shared_task\n> not updated + token unchanged + assignment now held by B.\" Pin TS2's observable end-state with the public\n> repo surface + 205's in-module test as the unit proof. TS2 (SC3): a partition cannot cause double execution — stale-token commit is rejected.\nuse sqlx::PgPool;\nuse remote::db::task_assignments::TaskAssignmentRepository;\n\nfn database_url() -> Option<String> { std::env::var(\"DATABASE_URL\").ok() }\nmacro_rules! skip_without_db { () => {\n    if database_url().is_none() { eprintln!(\"Skipping: DATABASE_URL not set\"); return; }\n}; }\nasync fn create_pool() -> PgPool { PgPool::connect(&database_url().unwrap()).await.expect(\"connect\") }\n// … inline create_test_organization / create_test_node + seed (task_id, node_project_id).\n\n#[tokio::test]\nasync fn partitioned_node_late_commit_is_rejected_after_reassignment() {\n    skip_without_db!();\n    let pool = create_pool().await;\n    let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n    // 1. Lease task T to node A (token T1). Use an already-past TTL to simulate the partition window.\n    let a = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(-1))\n        .await.unwrap().expect(\"A wins\");\n    // 2. A is partitioned-but-alive. The lease-expiry SWEEP (209) reclaims the expired lease, bumping the\n    //    token (exercises reclaim_expired_leases — why 210 depends_on 209). Then reassign to node B.\n    let reclaimed = repo.reclaim_expired_leases().await.unwrap();\n    assert!(reclaimed.iter().any(|r| r.task_id == task_id), \"the sweep reclaimed A's expired lease\");\n    let b = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_b, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n        .await.unwrap().expect(\"B claims the reclaimed task\");\n    assert!(b.fencing_token > a.fencing_token, \"B's token is strictly higher (partition-safety basis)\");\n    // 3. A's late commit (stamped with the OLD token T1) is STALE vs the assignment's current token T2.\n    //    Drive it through the seam 205 exposes (see scope note) and assert:\n    //      - the shared_task is NOT updated by A's stale op,\n    //      - the assignment's current fencing_token is STILL T2 (A's op did not roll it back),\n    //      - the rejection is surfaced (LeaseRevoked for A / an error) — A learns its lease is gone.\n    //    => at-most-once COMMIT effect: only the rightful holder (B, token T2) can commit.\n    let _ = (a, b);\n}\n```\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY create the one `tests/lease_partition_e2e.rs` integration test. skip_without_db { () => {\n        if database_url().is_none() { eprintln!(\"Skipping: DATABASE_URL not set\"); return; }\n    }; }\n    async fn create_pool() -> sqlx::PgPool {\n        sqlx::PgPool::connect(&database_url().unwrap()).await.expect(\"connect\")\n    }\n    // … inline create_test_organization / create_test_node and seed a (task_id, node_project_id) exactly\n    //    as backfill_e2e seeds them; produce a fresh `task_id: Uuid` per test for isolation.\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn try_claim_wins_when_available_and_assigns_monotonic_token() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        // seed org, node_a, task_id, node_project_id.\n        let claim = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, node_project_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(30))\n            .await.unwrap();\n        let claim = claim.expect(\"claim should succeed on an available task\");\n        assert_eq!(claim.node_id, node_a);\n        assert!(claim.fencing_token > 0, \"a granted token is from nextval (>0)\");\n        assert!(claim.lease_expires_at > chrono::Utc::now(), \"lease expiry is in the future\");\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn try_claim_fails_for_a_second_node_while_lease_is_live() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        // node_a claims with a long TTL.\n        let first = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        // node_b tries the SAME task while a's lease is live → None (no row updated, no double-claim).\n        let second = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_b, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n            .await.unwrap();\n        assert!(second.is_none(), \"a live lease blocks a second claimant\");\n        let _ = first;\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn try_claim_reclaims_an_expired_lease_with_a_strictly_higher_token() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        // node_a claims with a NEGATIVE TTL so lease_expires_at is already in the past.\n        let a = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(-1))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        // node_b now claims the EXPIRED lease → succeeds with a strictly higher token.\n        let b = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_b, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"b reclaims expired\");\n        assert_eq!(b.node_id, node_b);\n        assert!(b.fencing_token > a.fencing_token,\n            \"a reassigned lease MUST get a strictly higher fencing token (the SC3 basis)\");\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn renew_lease_extends_expiry_without_changing_the_token() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        let a = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(30))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        let renewed = repo.renew_lease(a.assignment_id, node_a, chrono::Duration::seconds(120))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"renew succeeds for the lease holder\");\n        assert_eq!(renewed.fencing_token, a.fencing_token, \"renew does NOT bump the token\");\n        assert!(renewed.lease_expires_at > a.lease_expires_at, \"renew extends the expiry\");\n        // a foreign node cannot renew someone else's lease.\n        let stolen = repo.renew_lease(a.assignment_id, node_b, chrono::Duration::seconds(120))\n            .await.unwrap();\n        assert!(stolen.is_none(), \"renew is scoped to the current lease holder\");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Change\n- **File:** `crates/remote/src/db/task_assignments.rs`\n- **Anchor:** add two methods inside `impl<'a> TaskAssignmentRepository<'a>` — place `try_claim` after\n  `create` Succeeds (returns Some) only when the task has NO live assignment:\n    /// either no active row, or the active row's lease has expired. Each grant bumps the monotonic\n    /// fencing token via nextval, so a reassigned lease always outranks any prior holder. Two nodes\n    /// can never both win (the UPDATE … RETURNING is atomic under the row lock). Returns None when a\n    /// live lease blocks the claim.\n    pub async fn try_claim(\n        &self,\n        task_id: Uuid,\n        node_id: Uuid,\n        node_project_id: Uuid,\n        lease_ttl: chrono::Duration,\n    ) -> Result<Option<LeaseClaim>, TaskAssignmentError> {\n        // CONTRACT (executor finalizes the exact statement(s) against the live schema):\n        //  - UPDATE the active row IFF it is reclaimable:\n        //      WHERE task_id = $1 AND completed_at IS NULL\n        //            AND (lease_expires_at IS NULL OR lease_expires_at < now())\n        //      SET node_id = $2, node_project_id = $3,\n        //          lease_expires_at = now() + ($interval from lease_ttl),\n        //          fencing_token = nextval('node_fencing_token_seq')\n        //      RETURNING id, node_id, task_id, fencing_token, lease_expires_at\n        //  - if 0 rows updated AND no active row exists at all → INSERT a fresh assignment with\n        //    lease_expires_at = now()+ttl and fencing_token = nextval(...) (same RETURNING).\n","metadata":{"output":"    },\n    /// Lease revoked: the hive reclaimed/expired this assignment; the node must self-fence (SC3).\n    #[serde(rename = \"lease_revoked\")]\n    LeaseRevoked { assignment_id: Uuid, reason: String },\n}\n```\n- **Node `handle_hive_message` — add explicit `LeaseGrant` + `LeaseRevoked` STUB arms BEFORE the `_ =>`\n  wildcard @1062:**\n  - **Before (@1062-1064):**\n```rust\n            _ => {\n                tracing::debug!(?hive_msg, \"ignoring unhandled hive message\");\n            }\n```\n  - **After:**\n```rust\n            HiveMessage::LeaseGrant { assignment_id, fencing_token, lease_expires_at } => {\n                // STUB — filled by task 206 (store token+lease, emit HiveEvent::LeaseGranted). skip_without_db { () => {\n        if database_url().is_none() { eprintln!(\"Skipping: DATABASE_URL not set\"); return; }\n    }; }\n    async fn create_pool() -> sqlx::PgPool {\n as backfill_e2e seeds them; produce a fresh `task_id: Uuid` per test for isolation.\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn try_claim_wins_when_available_and_assigns_monotonic_token() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        // seed org, node_a, task_id, node_project_id.\n        let claim = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, node_project_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(30))\n            .await.unwrap();\n        let claim = claim.expect(\"claim should succeed on an available task\");\n        assert_eq!(claim.node_id, node_a);\n        assert!(claim.fencing_token > 0, \"a granted token is from nextval (>0)\");\n        assert!(claim.lease_expires_at > chrono::Utc::now(), \"lease expiry is in the future\");\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn try_claim_fails_for_a_second_node_while_lease_is_live() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        // node_a claims with a long TTL.\n        let first = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        // node_b tries the SAME task while a's lease is live → None (no row updated, no double-claim).\n        let second = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_b, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n            .await.unwrap();\n        assert!(second.is_none(), \"a live lease blocks a second claimant\");\n        let _ = first;\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn try_claim_reclaims_an_expired_lease_with_a_strictly_higher_token() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        // node_a claims with a NEGATIVE TTL so lease_expires_at is already in the past.\n        let a = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(-1))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        // node_b now claims the EXPIRED lease → succeeds with a strictly higher token.\n        let b = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_b, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(300))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"b reclaims expired\");\n        assert_eq!(b.node_id, node_b);\n renew_lease_extends_expiry_without_changing_the_token() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        let repo = TaskAssignmentRepository::new(&pool);\n        let a = repo.try_claim(task_id, node_a, np_id, chrono::Duration::seconds(30))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"a wins\");\n        let renewed = repo.renew_lease(a.assignment_id, node_a, chrono::Duration::seconds(120))\n            .await.unwrap().expect(\"renew succeeds for the lease holder\");\n        assert_eq!(renewed.fencing_token, a.fencing_token, \"renew does NOT bump the token\");\n        assert!(renewed.lease_expires_at > a.lease_expires_at, \"renew extends the expiry\");\n        // a foreign node cannot renew someone else's lease.\n        let stolen = repo.renew_lease(a.assignment_id, node_b, chrono::Duration::seconds(120))\n            .await.unwrap();\n        assert!(stolen.is_none(), \"renew is scoped to the current lease holder\");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Change\n- **File:** `crates/remote/src/db/task_assignments.rs`\n- **Anchor:** add two methods inside `impl<'a> TaskAssignmentRepository<'a>` — place `try_claim` after\n  `create` The lease fields live ON `ActiveAssignment` in `NodeRunnerState` (NOT a separate store — see Change),\nso the test exercises the grant/revoke effect on that map:\n```rust\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod lease_state_tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn lease_grant_sets_token_and_expiry_on_active_assignment_then_revoke_clears() {\n        let state = std::sync::Arc::new(tokio::sync::RwLock::new(NodeRunnerState::default()));\n        let aid = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        let local = uuid::Uuid::new_v4();\n        // Seed an active assignment (as HiveEvent::TaskAssigned would).\n        state.write().await.active_assignments.insert(aid, ActiveAssignment {\n            assignment_id: aid, task_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4(), local_task_id: Some(local),\n            local_attempt_id: None, status: TaskExecutionStatus::Pending,\n            fencing_token: None, lease_expires_at: None,\n        });\n        let expires = chrono::Utc::now() + chrono::Duration::seconds(60);\n\n        // apply_lease_grant is the small helper the process_event arm calls (testable, no WS).\n        apply_lease_grant(&state, aid, 7, expires).await;\n        {\n            let s = state.read().await;\n            let a = s.active_assignments.get(&aid).unwrap();\n            assert_eq!(a.fencing_token, Some(7));\n            assert_eq!(a.lease_expires_at, Some(expires));\n        }\n        // A higher token replaces a lower one; a grant never lowers a token.\n        apply_lease_grant(&state, aid, 9, expires).await;\n        assert_eq!(state.read().await.active_assignments.get(&aid).unwrap().fencing_token, Some(9));\n\n        apply_lease_revoke(&state, aid).await;\n        assert_eq!(state.read().await.active_assignments.get(&aid).unwrap().fencing_token, None);\n    }\n}\n```\n> Match `TaskExecutionStatus`'s real variant name (read it; the literal above is illustrative). Add the new\n  method beside it.\n- **Before:** (no `peek_from_seq` method exists)\n- **After:** add (NOTE: NO `acked_at IS NULL` filter — the whole point is to replay acked rows too):\n```rust\n    /// Re-stream ops for SC5 anti-entropy heal: all ops with `seq >= from_seq` in seq order, **including\n    /// already-acked ones** (a node-has/hive-lacks divergence means an acked op was lost hive-side, so it\n    /// MUST be replayable). Distinct from `peek_unacked`, which filters `acked_at IS NULL`. Safe to\n    /// over-send: the hive apply is idempotent (`ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`, 106) so re-streamed ops never\n    /// double-apply or re-advance falsely.\n    pub async fn peek_from_seq(\n        pool: &SqlitePool,\n        from_seq: i64,\n        limit: i64,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<OutboxOp>, sqlx::Error> {\n        let rows = sqlx::query!(\n            r#\"SELECT id as \"id!: Uuid\", seq as \"seq!: i64\", op_type, entity_type,\n                      entity_id as \"entity_id!: Uuid\", payload,\n                      idempotency_key, fencing_token as \"fencing_token: i64\",\n                      created_at as \"created_at!: DateTime<Utc>\",\n                      acked_at as \"acked_at: DateTime<Utc>\"\n               FROM node_outbox\n               WHERE seq >= ?\n               ORDER BY seq ASC\n               LIMIT ?\"#,\n            from_seq,\n            limit\n        )\n        .fetch_all(pool)\n        .await?;\n        rows.into_iter()\n            .map(|r| {\n                Ok(OutboxOp {\n                    id: r.id,\n                    seq: r.seq,\n                    op_type: r.op_type,\n                    entity_type: r.entity_type,\n                    entity_id: r.entity_id,\n                    payload: serde_json::from_str(&r.payload).unwrap_or(serde_json::Value::Null),\n                    idempotency_key: r.idempotency_key,\n                    fencing_token: r.fencing_token,\n                    created_at: r.created_at,\n                    acked_at: r.acked_at,\n                })\n            })\n            .collect()\n    }\n```\n> Match 104's EXACT select-cast + payload-parse style (read 104's `peek_unacked` and copy it, dropping\n> only the `WHERE acked_at IS NULL` and changing it to `WHERE seq >= ?`). It does **not** touch Postgres,\ndoes **not** call a `query!`/`query_as!`, and does **not** stand up a node↔hive socket. There is NO\n`skip_without_db!` guard because there is no DB precondition — the test runs and passes (or fails to\ncompile) on any checkout. Do NOT add a `DATABASE_URL` precondition; doing so would make a hermetic\nguard look like the skip-guarded hive tests and invite a hollow pass.\n\n**Why this is the right shape (the invariant restated).** SC1's data-plane half is \"no node↔node /\nnode↔hive↔node fan-out\": a shared task owned by node X is never *pushed* to a different node Y. The hive\ndelivers `HiveMessage` to nodes by exactly four send primitives in\n`crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs` — `send_to_node` (123), `broadcast_to_org` (138),\n`broadcast_to_org_except` (159), `send_to_nodes` (189) — plus per-node direct replies via\n`send_message` in `session.rs`. The invariant is structural: **every variant of `HiveMessage` is either\n(a) a per-node control/handshake/ack reply, (b) the *recipient's own* assignment/cancel, (c) the\n*recipient's own* backfill request, or (d) project/label *metadata* — and NONE carries another node's\nshared-*task* state for relay to a third party.** A future variant that pushed shared task state would\nhave to be added to `HiveMessage`, and this test forces that addition to be classified (via an\nexhaustive `match`) and then asserts the classification contains no `TaskStatePush`. That is the\nregression fence: you cannot add a fan-out variant without either (i) editing this test's `match` (which\nmakes the intent reviewable) or (ii) breaking the build (non-exhaustive match under `-D warnings`).\n\n**The test MUST be a NEW integration test file** `crates/remote/tests/no_fanout_invariant.rs`.\n`HiveMessage` is `pub` and reachable as `vks_hive_server::nodes::ws::message::HiveMessage`\n(crate name is `vks-hive-server`; `nodes`, `ws`, `message` are all `pub mod`). An external integration\ntest sees it. **Sibling read (rubric #9):** `crates/remote/tests/pool_config.rs` is the existing\n*hermetic* (no-DB) integration test in this dir — copy its bare `use vks_hive_server::…;` + `#[test]`\nshape (NOT `backfill_e2e.rs`, which is the DB-bound template and the wrong model here).\n\nCreate `crates/remote/tests/no_fanout_invariant.rs` with EXACTLY this content:\n```rust\n//! SC1 data-plane guard — no node↔node / node↔hive↔node fan-out.\n//!\n//! Asserts the structural invariant that the node-facing channel (`HiveMessage`,\n//! the ONLY thing a node can receive) never carries one node's shared-*task* state\n//! for relay to a different node. The exhaustive `match` below is a regression\n//! fence: a new `HiveMessage` variant cannot be added without classifying it here,\n//! and the test rejects any classification of `TaskStatePush`.\n//!\n//! Pairs with the send-site comment fence in\n//! `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs` (task 602).\n\nuse vks_hive_server::nodes::ws::message::{\n    AuthResultMessage, BackfillRequestMessage, BackfillType, HiveMessage, LabelSyncBroadcastMessage,\n    NodeRemovedMessage, ProjectSyncMessage, TaskAssignMessage, TaskCancelMessage, TaskDetails,\n    TaskSyncResponseMessage,\n};\n\n/// How a `HiveMessage` reaches a node — the allowed delivery classes for SC1.\n#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Eq)]\nenum Delivery {\n    /// Per-node handshake / control / ack reply on the recipient's OWN socket\n    /// (auth_result, heartbeat_ack, status_request, error, close, task_sync_response).\n    PerNodeControl,\n    /// The recipient's OWN assignment or cancel of its OWN assignment.\n    OwnAssignment,\n    /// A request for the recipient to push ITS OWN data up to the hive (carries no task state).\n    OwnBackfillRequest,\n    /// Project METADATA (link id, repo path, branch, owner-node display) — NOT shared-task state.\n    ProjectMetadata,\n    /// Organization-global label metadata broadcast (label name/icon/color/version) — NOT task state.\n    LabelMetadata,\n    /// FORBIDDEN: a push of one node's shared-TASK state to a different node. No variant may map here.\n    /// Present only so the assertion below is meaningful; if a future variant is task-state fan-out,\n    /// classify it here and watch this test fail (that is the point).\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    TaskStatePush,\n}\n\n/// Total, exhaustive classification of every `HiveMessage` variant. Adding a variant without\n/// extending this `match` fails to compile under `-D warnings` — the regression fence.\nfn classify(msg: &HiveMessage) -> Delivery {\n    match msg {\n        HiveMessage::AuthResult(_) => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::HeartbeatAck { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::StatusRequest { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::Error { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::Close { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::TaskSyncResponse(_) => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::TaskAssign(_) => Delivery::OwnAssignment,\n        HiveMessage::TaskCancel(_) => Delivery::OwnAssignment,\n        HiveMessage::BackfillRequest(_) => Delivery::OwnBackfillRequest,\n        HiveMessage::ProjectSync(_) => Delivery::ProjectMetadata,\n        HiveMessage::NodeRemoved(_) => Delivery::ProjectMetadata,\n        HiveMessage::LabelSync(_) => Delivery::LabelMetadata,\n        // Added by P1 task 103 (this task `depends_on: 103`, so OpAck is present at execution time):\n        // durable ack on the recipient's OWN op-log cursor — control, never task-state fan-out.\n        HiveMessage::OpAck { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        // If P2/P5 have also landed, add their decision-locked arms here (see the table above).\n        // Use the variant's ACTUAL shape from message.rs — per CONTRACT §A these are struct-variants,\n        // and DigestResult is `DigestResult { .. }` (P5 task 501), so match with `{ .. }` not `(_)`:\n        //   HiveMessage::LeaseGrant { .. } | HiveMessage::LeaseRevoked { .. } => Delivery::OwnAssignment,\n        //   HiveMessage::DigestResult { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        // and a matching constructor in one_of_each(). They are NOT on main and may not exist yet.\n    }\n}\n\nfn sample_uuid() -> uuid::Uuid {\n    uuid::Uuid::nil()\n}\n\n/// One representative value per `HiveMessage` variant. This forces every variant to be CONSTRUCTED\n/// here, so renaming/removing a variant breaks this list (a second fence alongside `classify`).\nfn one_of_each() -> Vec<HiveMessage> {\n    let now = chrono::Utc::now();\n    vec![\n        HiveMessage::AuthResult(AuthResultMessage {\n            success: true,\n            node_id: Some(sample_uuid()),\n            organization_id: Some(sample_uuid()),\n            error: None,\n            protocol_version: 1,\n            linked_projects: vec![],\n            swarm_labels: vec![],\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::HeartbeatAck { server_time: now },\n        HiveMessage::StatusRequest { message_id: sample_uuid() },\n        HiveMessage::Error { message_id: None, error: \"x\".into() },\n        HiveMessage::Close { reason: \"x\".into() },\n        HiveMessage::TaskSyncResponse(TaskSyncResponseMessage {\n            local_task_id: sample_uuid(),\n            shared_task_id: sample_uuid(),\n            success: true,\n            error: None,\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::TaskAssign(TaskAssignMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            assignment_id: sample_uuid(),\n            task_id: sample_uuid(),\n            node_project_id: sample_uuid(),\n            local_project_id: sample_uuid(),\n            task: TaskDetails {\n                title: \"t\".into(),\n                description: None,\n                executor: \"CLAUDE_CODE\".into(),\n                executor_variant: None,\n                base_branch: \"main\".into(),\n            },\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::TaskCancel(TaskCancelMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            assignment_id: sample_uuid(),\n            reason: None,\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::BackfillRequest(BackfillRequestMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            backfill_type: BackfillType::FullAttempt,\n            entity_ids: vec![],\n            logs_after: None,\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::ProjectSync(ProjectSyncMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            link_id: sample_uuid(),\n            project_id: sample_uuid(),\n            project_name: \"p\".into(),\n            local_project_id: sample_uuid(),\n            git_repo_path: \"/r\".into(),\n            default_branch: \"main\".into(),\n A task owned by node X is never relayed to node Y as task state; the\n/// only task-shaped variants (`TaskAssign`/`TaskSyncResponse`) are the recipient's OWN assignment /\n/// its OWN sync ack, classified as `OwnAssignment` / `PerNodeControl`, never `TaskStatePush`.\n#[test]\nfn no_hive_message_variant_is_task_state_fanout() {\n    for msg in one_of_each() {\n        let class = classify(&msg);\n        assert_ne!(\n            class,\n            Delivery::TaskStatePush,\n            \"HiveMessage variant {msg:?} classified as forbidden TaskStatePush fan-out — \\\n             SC1 no-fanout invariant violated. If this is a legitimate new control/assignment/\\\n             metadata variant, classify it accordingly; a task-state push to nodes is OUT of \\\n             scope (the hive UI reads Postgres directly).\"\n        );\n    }\n}\n```\n> Run before the change exists: `cargo test -p vks-hive-server --test no_fanout_invariant` — RED\n> (the file does not compile/exist). It does **not** touch Postgres,\ndoes **not** call a `query!`/`query_as!`, and does **not** stand up a node↔hive socket. There is NO\n`skip_without_db!` guard because there is no DB precondition — the test runs and passes (or fails to\ncompile) on any checkout. Do NOT add a `DATABASE_URL` precondition; doing so would make a hermetic\nguard look like the skip-guarded hive tests and invite a hollow pass.\n\n**Why this is the right shape (the invariant restated).** SC1's data-plane half is \"no node↔node /\nnode↔hive↔node fan-out\": a shared task owned by node X is never *pushed* to a different node Y. The hive\ndelivers `HiveMessage` to nodes by exactly four send primitives in\n`crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs` — `send_to_node` (123), `broadcast_to_org` (138),\n`broadcast_to_org_except` (159), `send_to_nodes` (189) — plus per-node direct replies via\n`send_message` in `session.rs`. The invariant is structural: **every variant of `HiveMessage` is either\n(a) a per-node control/handshake/ack reply, (b) the *recipient's own* assignment/cancel, (c) the\n*recipient's own* backfill request, or (d) project/label *metadata* — and NONE carries another node's\nshared-*task* state for relay to a third party.** A future variant that pushed shared task state would\nhave to be added to `HiveMessage`, and this test forces that addition to be classified (via an\nexhaustive `match`) and then asserts the classification contains no `TaskStatePush`. That is the\nregression fence: you cannot add a fan-out variant without either (i) editing this test's `match` (which\nmakes the intent reviewable) or (ii) breaking the build (non-exhaustive match under `-D warnings`).\n\n**The test MUST be a NEW integration test file** `crates/remote/tests/no_fanout_invariant.rs`.\n`HiveMessage` is `pub` and reachable as `vks_hive_server::nodes::ws::message::HiveMessage`\n(crate name is `vks-hive-server`; `nodes`, `ws`, `message` are all `pub mod`). An external integration\ntest sees it. **Sibling read (rubric #9):** `crates/remote/tests/pool_config.rs` is the existing\n*hermetic* (no-DB) integration test in this dir — copy its bare `use vks_hive_server::…;` + `#[test]`\nshape (NOT `backfill_e2e.rs`, which is the DB-bound template and the wrong model here).\n\nCreate `crates/remote/tests/no_fanout_invariant.rs` with EXACTLY this content:\n```rust\n//! SC1 data-plane guard — no node↔node / node↔hive↔node fan-out.\n//!\n//! Asserts the structural invariant that the node-facing channel (`HiveMessage`,\n//! the ONLY thing a node can receive) never carries one node's shared-*task* state\n//! for relay to a different node. The exhaustive `match` below is a regression\n//! fence: a new `HiveMessage` variant cannot be added without classifying it here,\n//! and the test rejects any classification of `TaskStatePush`.\n//!\n//! Pairs with the send-site comment fence in\n//! `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs` (task 602).\n\nuse vks_hive_server::nodes::ws::message::{\n    AuthResultMessage, BackfillRequestMessage, BackfillType, HiveMessage, LabelSyncBroadcastMessage,\n    NodeRemovedMessage, ProjectSyncMessage, TaskAssignMessage, TaskCancelMessage, TaskDetails,\n    TaskSyncResponseMessage,\n};\n\n/// How a `HiveMessage` reaches a node — the allowed delivery classes for SC1.\n#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Eq)]\nenum Delivery {\n    /// Per-node handshake / control / ack reply on the recipient's OWN socket\n    /// (auth_result, heartbeat_ack, status_request, error, close, task_sync_response).\n    PerNodeControl,\n    /// The recipient's OWN assignment or cancel of its OWN assignment.\n    OwnAssignment,\n    /// A request for the recipient to push ITS OWN data up to the hive (carries no task state).\n    OwnBackfillRequest,\n    /// Project METADATA (link id, repo path, branch, owner-node display) — NOT shared-task state.\n    ProjectMetadata,\n    /// Organization-global label metadata broadcast (label name/icon/color/version) — NOT task state.\n    LabelMetadata,\n    /// FORBIDDEN: a push of one node's shared-TASK state to a different node. No variant may map here.\n    /// Present only so the assertion below is meaningful; if a future variant is task-state fan-out,\n    /// classify it here and watch this test fail (that is the point).\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    TaskStatePush,\n}\n\n/// Total, exhaustive classification of every `HiveMessage` variant. Adding a variant without\n/// extending this `match` fails to compile under `-D warnings` — the regression fence.\nfn classify(msg: &HiveMessage) -> Delivery {\n    match msg {\n        HiveMessage::AuthResult(_) => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::HeartbeatAck { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::StatusRequest { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::Error { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::Close { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::TaskSyncResponse(_) => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        HiveMessage::TaskAssign(_) => Delivery::OwnAssignment,\n        HiveMessage::TaskCancel(_) => Delivery::OwnAssignment,\n        HiveMessage::BackfillRequest(_) => Delivery::OwnBackfillRequest,\n        HiveMessage::ProjectSync(_) => Delivery::ProjectMetadata,\n        HiveMessage::NodeRemoved(_) => Delivery::ProjectMetadata,\n        HiveMessage::LabelSync(_) => Delivery::LabelMetadata,\n        // Added by P1 task 103 (this task `depends_on: 103`, so OpAck is present at execution time):\n        // durable ack on the recipient's OWN op-log cursor — control, never task-state fan-out.\n        HiveMessage::OpAck { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        // If P2/P5 have also landed, add their decision-locked arms here (see the table above).\n        // Use the variant's ACTUAL shape from message.rs — per CONTRACT §A these are struct-variants,\n        // and DigestResult is `DigestResult { .. }` (P5 task 501), so match with `{ .. }` not `(_)`:\n        //   HiveMessage::LeaseGrant { .. } | HiveMessage::LeaseRevoked { .. } => Delivery::OwnAssignment,\n        //   HiveMessage::DigestResult { .. } => Delivery::PerNodeControl,\n        // and a matching constructor in one_of_each(). They are NOT on main and may not exist yet.\n    }\n}\n\nfn sample_uuid() -> uuid::Uuid {\n    uuid::Uuid::nil()\n}\n\n/// One representative value per `HiveMessage` variant. This forces every variant to be CONSTRUCTED\n/// here, so renaming/removing a variant breaks this list (a second fence alongside `classify`).\nfn one_of_each() -> Vec<HiveMessage> {\n    let now = chrono::Utc::now();\n    vec![\n        HiveMessage::AuthResult(AuthResultMessage {\n            success: true,\n            node_id: Some(sample_uuid()),\n            organization_id: Some(sample_uuid()),\n            error: None,\n            protocol_version: 1,\n            linked_projects: vec![],\n            swarm_labels: vec![],\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::HeartbeatAck { server_time: now },\n        HiveMessage::StatusRequest { message_id: sample_uuid() },\n        HiveMessage::Error { message_id: None, error: \"x\".into() },\n        HiveMessage::Close { reason: \"x\".into() },\n        HiveMessage::TaskSyncResponse(TaskSyncResponseMessage {\n            local_task_id: sample_uuid(),\n            shared_task_id: sample_uuid(),\n            success: true,\n            error: None,\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::TaskAssign(TaskAssignMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            assignment_id: sample_uuid(),\n              description: None,\n                executor: \"CLAUDE_CODE\".into(),\n                executor_variant: None,\n                base_branch: \"main\".into(),\n            },\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::TaskCancel(TaskCancelMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            assignment_id: sample_uuid(),\n            reason: None,\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::BackfillRequest(BackfillRequestMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            backfill_type: BackfillType::FullAttempt,\n            entity_ids: vec![],\n            logs_after: None,\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::ProjectSync(ProjectSyncMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            link_id: sample_uuid(),\n            project_id: sample_uuid(),\n            project_name: \"p\".into(),\n            local_project_id: sample_uuid(),\n            git_repo_path: \"/r\".into(),\n            default_branch: \"main\".into(),\n            source_node_id: sample_uuid(),\n            source_node_name: \"n\".into(),\n            source_node_public_url: None,\n            is_new: true,\n        }),\n        HiveMessage::NodeRemoved(NodeRemovedMessage {\n            node_id: sample_uuid(),\n            reason: \"x\".into(),\n        }),\n        // P1 task 103 variant (present because this task depends_on If 103's payload shape\n        // differs from CONTRACT §A `{ applied_through_seq: i64 }`, build from the actual variant.\n        HiveMessage::OpAck { applied_through_seq: 0 },\n        HiveMessage::LabelSync(LabelSyncBroadcastMessage {\n            message_id: sample_uuid(),\n            shared_label_id: sample_uuid(),\n            project_id: None,\n            origin_node_id: sample_uuid(),\n            name: \"l\".into(),\n            icon: \"tag\".into(),\n            color: \"#fff\".into(),\n            version: 1,\n            is_deleted: false,\n        }),\n    ]\n}\n\n/// TS7 — no fan-out: NO `HiveMessage` variant the hive can deliver to a node is a push of another\n/// node's shared-TASK state. A task owned by node X is never relayed to node Y as task state; the\n/// only task-shaped variants (`TaskAssign`/`TaskSyncResponse`) are the recipient's OWN assignment /\n/// its OWN sync ack, classified as `OwnAssignment` / `PerNodeControl`, never `TaskStatePush`.\n#[test]\nfn no_hive_message_variant_is_task_state_fanout() {\n    for msg in one_of_each() {\n        let class = classify(&msg);\n        assert_ne!(\n            class,\n            Delivery::TaskStatePush,\n            \"HiveMessage variant {msg:?} classified as forbidden TaskStatePush fan-out — \\\n             SC1 no-fanout invariant violated. If this is a legitimate new control/assignment/\\\n             metadata variant, classify it accordingly; a task-state push to nodes is OUT of \\\n             scope (the hive UI reads Postgres directly).\"\n        );\n    }\n}\n```\n> Run before the change exists: `cargo test -p vks-hive-server --test no_fanout_invariant` — RED\n> (the file does not compile/exist). Both crates' enums\n(node `task/mod.rs:27`, hive `tasks.rs:25`) are exactly `Todo/InProgress/InReview/Done/Cancelled` — there\nis **no `Failed`, no `Assigned`** variant. SC4's parenthetical `assigned`/`failed` are authority labels\nfor lifecycle concepts that map to OTHER columns, not `task.status` values: `assigned` = an active\n`node_task_assignments` row (hive, assignment layer, ADR-0009); `failed` = an `execution_status` outcome\n(node, execution layer). The ratified `task.status` matrix encoded below:\n- **Hive-authored:** `Todo→InProgress` (the on-assign-and-start transition), `InReview→Done` /\n  `InReview→InProgress` (operator review), `*→Cancelled` (operator action).\n- **Node-reported** (accepted only with a valid lease + current fencing token — 303 enforces):\n  `InProgress→InReview`, `InProgress→Done`.\n\nThis matrix, 303's TS3 enforcement, and 304's legacy-path mapping are all encoded against these ratified\nvalues. See `dev-docs/adr/0010-task-status-state-machine.md` (## Decision).\n\n## Failing test (write first)\n**HERMETIC — NO Postgres.** This task is a pure transition table (an enum + two fns over the hive\n`TaskStatus`). It has NO DB, NO lease, NO fencing — those live in 303. Its test is a plain\n`#[cfg(test)] mod tests` with no `DATABASE_URL` precondition and NO fail-closed gate prefix (contrast 303,\nwhich IS Postgres-bound). Keeping the author-legality matrix out from behind a DB skip means it always runs.\n\nThe test lives INSIDE the new `status_machine.rs` (the fns are `pub(crate)`, the test is colocated):\n\n```rust\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use crate::db::tasks::TaskStatus;\n\n    // Every legal transition is accepted from its SOLE author; the other party is rejected.\n    #[test]\n    fn matrix_authors_each_transition_exactly_once() {\n        // table: (from, to, expected_author)\n        let cases: &[(TaskStatus, TaskStatus, TransitionAuthor)] = &[\n            // hive-authored lifecycle (over the hive enum's actual variants — the reconciled matrix)\n            (TaskStatus::InReview, TaskStatus::Done, TransitionAuthor::Hive), // operator approve\n            (TaskStatus::InReview, TaskStatus::InProgress, TransitionAuthor::Hive), // operator reopen\n            (TaskStatus::InProgress, TaskStatus::Cancelled, TransitionAuthor::Hive),\n            (TaskStatus::InReview, TaskStatus::Cancelled, TransitionAuthor::Hive),\n            (TaskStatus::Done, TaskStatus::Cancelled, TransitionAuthor::Hive),\n            // node-reported (rideable only with a valid lease+token — 303 enforces that; the matrix\n            // only declares the AUTHOR)\n            (TaskStatus::InProgress, TaskStatus::Done, TransitionAuthor::Node),\n            (TaskStatus::InProgress, TaskStatus::InReview, TransitionAuthor::Node),\n        ];\n        for (from, to, want) in cases {\n            assert_eq!(\n                author_of_transition(*from, *to),\n                Some(*want),\n                \"author of {:?}->{:?}\",\n                from,\n                to\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn illegal_transitions_have_no_author() {\n        // A transition not in the matrix is rejected (no author) — illegal, never merged.\n        assert_eq!(author_of_transition(TaskStatus::Done, TaskStatus::InProgress), None);\n        assert_eq!(author_of_transition(TaskStatus::Cancelled, TaskStatus::InProgress), None);\n        assert_eq!(author_of_transition(TaskStatus::Done, TaskStatus::InReview), None);\n        // a no-op (from == to) is not an authored transition\n        assert_eq!(author_of_transition(TaskStatus::Done, TaskStatus::Done), None);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn node_may_author_only_node_transitions() {\n        // The predicate 303 calls: may a NODE report author `from→to`?\n        assert!(node_may_author(TaskStatus::InProgress, TaskStatus::Done));\n        assert!(node_may_author(TaskStatus::InProgress, TaskStatus::InReview));\n        // a node may NOT author a hive transition (the core SC4 rejection)\n        assert!(!node_may_author(TaskStatus::InReview, TaskStatus::Done));\n        assert!(!node_may_author(TaskStatus::InReview, TaskStatus::InProgress));\n        assert!(!node_may_author(TaskStatus::InProgress, TaskStatus::Cancelled));\n        // no-op / illegal are not node-authored\n        assert!(!node_may_author(TaskStatus::Done, TaskStatus::Done));\n        assert!(!node_may_author(TaskStatus::Done, TaskStatus::InProgress));\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Change\n- **File:** `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/status_machine.rs` (NEW)\n- **Anchor:** whole file (create).\n- **Before:** (file does not exist)\n- **After:** a self-contained module encoding ADR-0010 §D over the hive `TaskStatus`\n  (`crate::db::tasks::TaskStatus` — `Todo/InProgress/InReview/Done/Cancelled`, `tasks.rs:25`). It declares\n  WHO authors each transition; it does NOT touch the DB, lease, or fencing.\n```rust\n//! Explicit `task.status` transition matrix (ADR-0010 §D, CONTRACT §D).\n//!\n//! Single source of truth for WHICH party may author WHICH status transition. Every legal\n//! transition has exactly ONE authoritative author, so there is no field-level status merge (SC4).\n//! This module is pure: it encodes the matrix and answers author/legality questions. Enforcement at\n//! the apply site (rejecting an illegal or wrong-author transition, and requiring a valid\n//! lease + fencing token for node-reported transitions) lives in `session.rs::handle_op_batch`\n//! (task 303), which rides P2's fencing check (CONTRACT §C).\n\nuse crate::db::tasks::TaskStatus;\n\n/// The party authorized to author a given status transition.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub(crate) enum TransitionAuthor {\n    /// Hive-authored (operator / assignment lifecycle): `todo→in-progress` (the on-assign-and-start\n    /// analog), `in-review→done` / `in-review→in-progress` (operator review), `*→cancelled`. (ADR-0010's\n    /// reconciled matrix collapses the `assigned` concept into the `node_task_assignments` row, not a\n    /// hive `TaskStatus` value — see the module/STOP note.)\n    Hive,\n    /// Node-reported up the outbox, accepted only with a valid lease + current fencing token (303):\n    /// `in-progress→done`, `in-progress→in-review`.\n    Node,\n}\n\n/// Return the sole authoritative author of `from → to`, or `None` if the transition is illegal\n/// (not in the matrix). A no-op (`from == to`) returns `None` — it is not an authored transition.\npub(crate) fn author_of_transition(from: TaskStatus, to: TaskStatus) -> Option<TransitionAuthor> {\n    use TaskStatus::*;\n    match (from, to) {\n        // hive-authored lifecycle\n        (Todo, InProgress) => Some(TransitionAuthor::Hive), // assign + start\n        (InReview, InProgress) => Some(TransitionAuthor::Hive), // operator reopen\n        (InReview, Done) => Some(TransitionAuthor::Hive), // operator approve\n        (_, Cancelled) if from != Cancelled => Some(TransitionAuthor::Hive),\n        // node-reported work/terminal transitions\n        (InProgress, Done) => Some(TransitionAuthor::Node),\n        (InProgress, InReview) => Some(TransitionAuthor::Node),\n        // everything else (incl. no-ops) is illegal\n        _ => None,\n    }\n}\n\n/// True iff a NODE report may author `from → to` (the predicate 303's enforcement calls before\n/// applying a node-reported status). False for hive-authored transitions, illegal transitions, and\n/// no-ops.\npub(crate) fn node_may_author(from: TaskStatus, to: TaskStatus) -> bool {\n    matches!(author_of_transition(from, to), Some(TransitionAuthor::Node))\n}\n```\n- **File:** `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/mod.rs`\n- **Anchor:** the module-declaration block (`ws/mod.rs:16-19`).\n- **Before:**\n```rust\nmod connection;\nmod dispatcher;\npub mod message;\nmod session;\n```\n- **After:**\n```rust\nmod connection;\nmod dispatcher;\npub mod message;\nmod session;\nmod status_machine;\n```\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY: create `status_machine.rs` with the enum + the two fns + the colocated `#[cfg(test)] mod tests`,\nand add the single `mod status_machine;` line to `ws/mod.rs`.
